PSALMA DHAIBHIDH A NMEADRACHD. Do reir an phriomh-chanamain. Le MA: RAIBEARD
KIRK, Minisdir SHOIGEIL CHRIOSD aig BALBHUIDIER. Maille re Ughdarras.

A bfuil neach gu dubhach inar measg? deanadh se urnaidh. Abfuil neach ar bioth
subhach? Sinnadh e Sailm. Ebisd: Sheum: Caibid. 5. Rann. 13. Ar a ngcur a ngelo
a nDun-Edin le M. Semus Kniblo, Joshua van Solingen agus Seon Colmar, 1684.

The Privilege.
FORASMVCH as there being an address made to the Lords of his Majesty's privy
Council, by Mr Robert Kirk minister at Balqwhidder, Bearing, that the
petitioner has been at great pains, diligence, and exactness in translating
the Psalms of David in Scottish-Irish meeter, which has hitherto been
endeavored by many, but never till now brought to perfection. And in regaird
the said translation, is approven by some of the Lords of the Clergy, and some
reverend Ministers who best understand the Irish-Language, as their approbation
more fully bears: Humbly Supplicating, That the Council would give order for
printing the said translation, and discharge all others from doing the same,
during such space as the Council should think fit. The said Lords having
considered the foresaid address, with a certificat under the hands of several
of the clergy, of the exactnes of the work of the said translation of the
Psalms into Scotish-Irish me^ter, and of the usefulnes of it for such as do
not understand the English translation; Do Approve of the petitioners great
care and pains: and of the said work done by him in perfecting the said
translation; And allow the same to be printed. And give and Grant to the
petitioner, his aires and assigneies, the sole power and privilege of printing
thereof: And Discharge all others so to do, for the space of eleven years after
the date hereof, under the pain of confiscation of the same to the Petitioner
and his foresaids use, and being further punished as the council shall find
cause. Extr. by me

Will. Paterson Cls. Sti: Con.
Edinb. 20. of March, 1684.
To the Potent and Renoun'd, Lord JOHN MURRAY, Marquess of ATHOLE, Earl of
Tullibardin, Viscount of Balquidder, Lord Murray and Balveny, Lord Keeper of
his Majesty Privy Seal, etc.
THE Matter of this Book, Most noble Marquess, sounded on inspired Writings,
needs no Defense, but a Metrical Translation of so Divine and rapturous a
Subject, into a language, not so much cultivate and polisht with Learning,
Oratory, and Divine poesy as need were; and done by such as attained not the
tongue without indefatigable industry, does require Religious, Equitable and
Generous persons to own it.

Your Noble self is patron of the place where the Translator officiats as a
Presbyter. You are now of the greatest Command among those that make use of
this Scotish-Irish Language on either side of the Grampian Mountains. Your
Lordship, has ever been of undoubted courage, and loyalty for the King; and
still along inflexible to the persuasions or Threats of frozen Newtralists or
Flaming incen diaries in Church or State. Your solid Moderation (a monument and
copy for succeeding Ages) in Disputable cases of Church Government and State
policy, with a constant regard to upright justice, and piety, has by the
providence of Heaven, occasioned your Lordships standing in what Reelings and
Revolutions have been: which was much furthered by your so Christian and
sagacious observance of our Saviors injunction anent the chief seats; In being
ever the Higher the Humbler. Were this public acknowledgment then to be
accounted of, it could no where be so aptly placed, and to none more worthily
ascribed then to your Noble sel^, of such merit in general, Besides my
particular Benefactor.

The Language being Vehicl of the more substantial part, I endeavored here
what was native and proper, but clean and plain for all capacities, shunning as
much as I could, tedious, tumultuous and disjoynted phrases. And tho I have
also s^ript some words of their superfluous and ^^^^ul^tory letters, reserving
the possessive, as the several Irish Grammers come to my hands, do allow; Yet
no humane work can pretend to be so absolute s to be beyond all Correction.
Notwithstanding, My Lord, it may be not unworthy the pains in every Age to
contribute a mite or two at least to the Churches Corban, For assisting of our
Sagacious Scot^sh Irish people in their public or private Devotions; speci^lly
seeing experience tells us that this their matern^l Tongue either in Ireland or
Scotland, is not easily abolisht by the contiguity and commixture of another
language: which no doubt is well understood by the present worthy and Laborious
Translators of the H. Bible in Irish.

In reference to such pious and laudable interprises your Lordship is looked
upon as ane Ebed-melech, to defend and encourage the Authors, that they be not
dismounted, and made to stagger from their post and province, because of the
tang of Atheism so much prevailing, the forlorn art of ridiculing with all
things, and many men's utter disdaining of what is not shapt in their own mould.
For the spiderweb of such polluted vanities, pompous and ultramundane fancy's,
in persons either courageously wicked, politickly profane, or monstruously
invidious. is too thin, not to be discovered by your Lordship, as it is by all
who love what is sober, and do not follow the guise of living in a desperate
Autonomy, flouting at all that is serious, adoring only the Idol they form to
themselv's, and not considering the end. Among others that thus presume on your
Lordships patrociny and candid acceptance, is one who implores the Divine
Conduct in this World, and Happiness in the next, to your Honurable Self and
all the branches of your Noble stem, and is still determined.

Most Noble Lord To serve your Lordship in all the Offices of Honor and Duty
M. R. Kirk.

Don' LEAGHCHORA, Since and Slainte.
ATaid na Psalma taitneamhach, tarbhach: ^eag nach mion-fhlaitheas lan
dainglibh, Cill fhonnmhar le ceol naomhtha. Mur abholghort Eden, lionta do
chrannuibh brioghmh^ire na ^eatha, and do lu^bhennibh jocs^lainteamhail,
amhleidh an leabhar Psalm so Dhaibhioth, ata na liagh^i^ ar uile anshocair na
nanma. Ata an saoghal and gach beo-chreatuir da bfuil ann, na chlarsigh: An du
ne, se is Clairseoir and duanaire, chum moladh an mor-Dhia mirbhuileach do
sh^inm; and ata Daibhidh do ghna mar fhear don chuideachd bhias marso ag
caoin-chaint gu ceolmhar ma nard. Ri.

Achd cheana, chum nach tuisleochadh tintiun ag leaghadh an 109. Salm, no
codcha da leitheid eile, Tuig nach caineadh no aoire na ndaoine is ciall
spioradalta dhoibh sud, achd guidheacha amhain anaghaidh eascairde na nanma,
bhias dar brosnughadh and dar breugnughadh chum ladh De chur a neimh-shuim.
Nior ghabh fos achd an ai^bfhiosach, Faighidheacht ar Judais no a chosmhul
eile, a riocht guidheacha coitchionda. ^s ceaduighteach ge ta, a jarraidh m^r
athchoinnidh ar Dhia, Began mirunn and mi-ghniomh luchd uilc a leigmhail ar
bhuil, anadhaidh na Heagluisi and na ngcreidmheacha: and taire sin a
fhuraileadh, Smachd seimh aims^ordha theachd ar an true, da cheartughadh, and
los gabhail roimh a sgriosadh siorraidh; amhuil do ni deagh-Jeremias air feign
C. 10. R. 24. Is dual fadheoigh, do na Firenibh na hinnil civil ata ainmnight
fna salmoibh, a thuigsinn ar gleus bhruideadh neamhdha, do chumhachdaibh
spioradadha an anam, chum Dia do ghlorughadh.

Do chuir sin an tsaothairse an uaim, a mbriathraibh scagtha, athehumair; ar
chomhbeag corrachus is a bfeidir linn. Gabhsa do tuaisle phrionnsamhail, mar
dheagh-fhlaith ghrianda, leithsgeul ar nuireasbhuidh, began bheith codarsna,
contrardha. Ni caire ar neach Dia dhonorughadh mur is fearr thig leis. Do
ghabhas mar chongnamh don obairsi, dioghlom ughdairidh an uile chail, ar
sheannos, phriomhchreideamh and eachdardha na n^aoidheal, sgriobhta and
clo-bhuailte: achd gu bareula juil and soluis dhamb, bri^h na nSalm feign. Anois
maseadh a Chomharbadha to chaomh, ata mar phlaneidi dhealroidh ag sdiurughadh
na ngcorp jochdardha began mhonmar, is deaghmhaise dhaoibh an tsaothairse a
sgrudadh and a ghnathughadh gu neimhf^iat, began ghuth ar bheiginmhe and
neimhnitheachd an^tsaothairigh. Griosam oraibhse a Vaisle, and a Thuatha
charthanacha araon, began bheith mur thacharain ar lua drean a nunn and a nall go
sbailpe breigi; achd le gcroidbihh daingne, dosgartha, deagh-fhreumhaighte,
druididh re Firinn, Ceart, and Ceannsachd, mar fhuraileas na psalma: Ata clu
and tarbha a nsdriocadh don choir; call and masla, a ntuitim le heugcoir.

Imthigh a Dhuilleachain gu dan,
Le Dan glan diagha duisg iad thall.
Cuir failte ar Fonn fial na bFionn,
Ar Gharbh chriocha, 's Indseadh gall.
PSALMA DHAIBHIDH A NMEADRACHD.
SALM. I.
BEANNUIGHT' an dujne sin nach gluais
a ngcomhairle na ndaoj,
Nach seas a nsligh' luchd uilc, 'san ait'
luchd fochaid fos nach suigh.
2. Achd a nlagh De da bfuil a thlachd,
ga smuaineadh oidhch is lo.
3. Bith se mur chraoibh ar suighiughadh
re taobh na naibhne mor,
Na haimsir jomchubhaidh bheir seach
a toradh pailt nar bfeadh,
Cha chrion a duille dhiobhail bridh;
gheibh soirbh gach ni ma ngabh.
4. Ni hamhluidh sin 'ta luchd an uilc,
achd mar an moll ataid,
Do fhuaduightear gach taobh le gaoi,
ga sgaoileadh ann sgach ait.
5. Bhridh sin cho seasamh na drochdhaoin'
san bhreathamhnas bhias ceart,
No peacaigh ann a ngcoimhthional
na mfircnidh, gu hait.
6. Ojr 'sfjosrach Dia air slighe ghloin
na mfirenidh a mfeast:
Achd fiar-sligh luchd na haingidheachd
dimhiltar i began cheist.
SALM II.
CREUD as far ghabh na cinnigh buil,
ag cruinniughadh gu borb,
'Sa mpobal creud far smuaintigh iad
beart dhiombaineach na lorg?
2. Rioghridh na cruinne a nordugh chuaidh,
'sna prionnsa chruinnigh siad,
Ghabh comhairle anadhaidh Dhia
'sa ^ungtha glan began bheud.
3. Ag radh, A ngcuibhreach brismid dh^nn,
is ^ilgmeid uainn a mboinn.
4. I^ia 'ta ar neamh na shuigh, ni gair'
is fanoid air na daoin'.
5. Sin labhraidh se na chorridh riu,
'sna lassan ruaigidh iad.
6. Gidheadh ar Sion mo chnoc naomh
oirn me mo righ na ait.
7. An torduigh nochdfuidh me gu ceart;
Dia mar do labhair riom
Is tu mo mhac, is ann a niugh
do gheineadh thusa leam.
8. Jarr orm, agus mar oighreachd ghlan
na cinnidh oheir me dhuic,
Criocha a ndomhain gheibh tu fos
na shealbha nach dteid uait.
9. Jad brisfidh tu gu mion began cheist
le slait don iaruinn chruaidh,
Mion-bhrudhaidh tu mar shoigheach cre.
is sgaoilfear leat na sloigh.
10. An^ois a riogha uime sin
grad ghlacaidh ciall na am:
A bhritheamhuin na talmhan fos
deagh-theagasg gabhaibh uam.
11. Le heagal adhraibh fos don Triath,
le ball-chrioth bithibh ait.
12 Is tugaibh pog don mhac le sailt
ar eagal shearg 'sa shlait;
Sgu gcaillfear sibh gu tur on rod
tra lasas fhearg achd beag:
Is beannuight iad gach ti gu brath
an dochas air do leag.
SALM III.
MO naimhde geur nach lionmhur iad,
'sna dheirigh riom a Dhe?
2. Is iomdha deir ma manam bochd
Dia air ni mfurtigh se.
3. Achd 'stu fear-togbhalach mo chinn,
mo sgia, 'smo ghloir gu caomh.
4. Do ghairmeas le mo ghuth air Dhia,
d'eist as a thuligh naomh.
5. Luigh, choidil, agus mhusguil me,
oir chum mo Dhia me suas.
6. Ni heagail leam deich mile sluaigh
do theachd fa mchuairt a nuas.
7. Dhe eirigh, Saor me O mo Dhia,
is tu do bhuail le neart
Mo naimhdeann uile ar a ngciall,
le dioghaltais to cheart,
Is bhris tu fiacla geur na ndaoi
8. 'Sle Dia an saoirse ait:
Do bheannachd air do phobul feign
a Dhe, 'ta ann sgach ait.
SALM IV.
EISD riom, os tu Dia mfhircantachd
san lo do ghairmfeas me:
Stu fhuasgujl orm is me a ndteinn,
foir orm, is eisd mo ghuidh.
2. Cia fhad do jompoigheadar mo ghloir
chum nair, O chlanna daoin?
Js bheir sibh gaol do dhiomhaineas,
ag rith re breugaibh baodha?
3. Bibh fiosrach gur thagh Dia o chach
an duine naomh, dho feign:
Sar-eisdeachd gheibh me fos o Dhia
tra ghairfeas air gu tren.
4. Biodh eagal oraibh, 'sna deanaibh lochd:
is ar bhur leapth' gu mor
Tiocfaidh ar smuainte glan le'r croidh',
'sbibh tostach mar is coir.
5. Deigh-iobairt cheartais jocalbh naibh
is earbfaidh ris an Triath.
6. Cia nochdfas duinne ein ni maith
'ta moran nois ag radha?
Dhia, tog oirn dealradh glan do ghnuis
7. Smo chuir tu dhaibhneas orm
No nuair budh lionmhur coirc is fion
a measg'na ngcinneach borb.
7. A nsithchaimh luidhidh me faraon,
is codlidh me began cheist:
Os tu bheir comhnuidh dhamh a Dhe
fuidh dhidean re a mfeast.
SALM V.
O Dhia, mo chainte toir fanear
is beachduigh air mo smuain.
2. Eisd guth mo ghlaodh, mo righ, smo Dhia,
oir guidheam ort gach uair.
3. San mhaidln cluinthear leat mo ghuth
a Thighearn' ann sgach cas;
Gu much do thogbham murnaidh riot,
is dearcam ortsa suas.
4. Cho tu an Dia ler' mian an tolc:
is lochd nj ncaidreann leat.
5. Luchd raithe a tfhiaghnais fos cho seas
fuadh leat luchd uilc gach neach.
6. Do sgrios far leat luchd labhradh breig:
is grain le Dia faraon
An duine fuileachdach, 'san ti
chum cealgoireachd do chlaon.
7. Achd mise, tiocfam chum do theach
thaoibh mead do ghrasa caoimh:
Is ann a teagal adhram dhuit,
maghaidh red' theampul naoimh.
8. Fachuis mo naimhde treoruigh me
ad cheartais naoimh, a Dhe.
Is deunsa romham ar gach ball
do chois-ceim direach re.
9. Na mbeul oir ni bfuil cinnt no ceart,
daor-aingidheachd a stigh,
An teangca, brionnach; fosgilt sos
a nscornan 'ta mar uaigh.
10. Grad-tuiteadar le ngcomhairlibh,
sgrios iad a Dhe gu goirt.
Na niomdha seachran fuaduigh iad,
oir rinnsiad ceannairc ort.
11. Achd lion da ndochas thu, biodh ait:
re gairdeachas do ghna
Os dion doibh thu; biodh aoibhneach dhiot
lion ghraidheas tainm gu brath.
12. Oir beanneodhair a nduine ceart:
le deagh-ghean fos a Dhe,
Ni tu a chuartughadh gu buan,
'sa dhionadh mar le sge.
SALM VI.
A Thighearna na cronidh me
ad' chorridh mhoir gu garg:
Na deun mo smachdughadh gu geur
an tan a lasas tfhearg.
2. Dean trocair orm a Dhia na ngras,
os lag ataim a nois;
Mo chnamban taid fa pheine ghoirt
a Thighearn' slanaidh mis.
3. Ta manam ar na chradh gu geur:
achd thus' cia fhad a Dhe,
4. Till, fuasgil manam; saor me feign
ar sgath do throcair re.
5. Oir ni bfuil cuimhne ort san bhas:
no bhuidhe riot 'sa nuaigh.
6. Ag cur mo leapth' ar snamh 'sa naoich,
'taim sgidh le mosnadh cruaidh:
Ma uirigh uisgeacham lem' dheoir.
7. Mo shuil chaith as le bron;
Arson muil' eascairdeadh ataim
ag dol gu haois is leon.
8. Nois teichibh uam, luchd uilc arfad,
oir chual mo Dhia mo chaoi.
9. Chual Dia guth m'athchoinnigh gu lua,
is gabhaidh uam mo ghuidh.
10. Gu dtigeadh nair is craghadh goirt
air meascairdeadh gu grad:
Beir orra dol le masladh dian
agcoinne a gcuil arfad.
SALM VII.
MO Dhia a Thighearn' earbfam riot
Saor me on druing gu leir
'Ta leanmhuin toir began adhbhar orm,
is furtigh orm gu tren.
2. Ar eagal mar ni leoghan allt'
gu reubfar manam leis
Ag deunamh liodairt dhe gu mion,
began fhear do fhuasgladh meis.
3. Ma dhearnas so a Dhia mo Thriath;
eugcoir a mlaimh ma ta:
4. Ma dhiol me olc don' fhear do bhi.
a nsithchaimh dhamh gach la:
(As gur be ni budh bheis leam feign
a theasrigin gu bla
Do bhi began adhbhar uam ar bith
na namhaid dhamh do ghna.)
5. Ruaigeadh an namhuid manam nois
ga ghlacadh, is gu lar
Saltradh mo bheatha, leagadh fos
m'onoir san uir le tar.
6. A ^tfheirg Dhe eirigh, tog feign suas
bhridh buil' mo naimhdeann garg.
Mosguil fam' chuis don' bhreitheamhnas
do orduigh thu na lorg
7. Mar sin nj coimhthional an tssuaigh
do chuartughadh began chaird;
Pfill uime sin fa ngcuis, is nochd
mordhachd a tionad ard.
8. Ni Dia, ceart chonbhail ris an tsluagh:
reir mjonnracais dean breith.
Js reir mo neimhchiontas a stigh
gu teann cuir as mo leith.
9. O tiocfadh crioch ar olc na ndaoj
achd daingnigh daojne ceart:
Oir rannsighidh gach croidh is ar
Dia comhthromach na mfeart.
10. Sar-sgia mo dhidin Dia ata,
dion dhaoine ceart a ngcroidh.
11. Bheir breath ar fireinidh, 'sgach lo
'ta feargach ris na daoi.
12. Ma seadh nach tillionn se ar ais
a chloidheamh liomhthar leis:
Air lagh a bhogha chuir gu teann
gu caitheamh, ullamh deas.
13. Fior-acsuin agus inneal marbha
do dheasigh ^e dho feign:
A shoighde do luchd diobhairgidh
do orduigh mar a gceudn:
14. Feuch, amhluidh mar bhios mnaoi re saothair,
re haingidheachd 'ta se:
An taimhleas se budh toirchios do,
breug rugadh leis gu re.
15. Do chlaoich se slochd, is threachail e,
na lag feign, thuit gu teann.
16. Thig aimhleas ar a chlaigceann feign
is shoirneart air a cheann.
17. Do reir a cheartais molaidh me
an Tighearna gach la
Do dhainm Jehobha sinnim clu
o se is airde 'ta.
PSALM VIII.
O Dhia ar Triath cia mordha tainm
ar feadh an tsaoghail gu leir?
Do ghloir do shocruigheas osciond
na mflaitheas is na nspeur.
2. As beul na naoidh 'sna ngciochran mao
bhridh teascar dorduigh neart
An namhuid chum gu gcoisgionn tu,
'san dioghaltach mi-cheart.
3. Do speura tra thug me fanear
oibridh do mheura grinn
An ghealach is na reulla fos
do orduigh thu gach linn;
4. Creud duine truagh gu gcuimhnis air,
no mhac gu fiosraigh tu?
5. Js beag nach dfuair se inmhe uait
mar fuair na haingil dlu.
Do chuir tu coroin aluin air
le mais is gloir gach lo.
6. Ar oibridh fos do laimh fud feign
deagh-uachdranachd thug dho*
Na duile chruthaigh thu a Dhe,
faoi chosaibh chuir gu leir.
7. Na caoirigh, buar, gach ajnmhidh fos
ag iomachd ar an fheur.
8. Na heunlaith 'ta san aidher shuas,
an tiasg ata san chuan,
Na shhiobhlas ar sligh fairrge moir
sin thugbhais do gu buan.
9. A Dhia ar Tighearna, cia maith,
cia uasal tainm feign?
Ar feadh an talmhuin fa gcuairt
is mor e mar a gcedn'.
SALM IX.
LE muile chroidh do bheirim dhuit
ardmholadh binn a Dhe;
Is toibridh mirbhuileach ar fad
do innsiom iad gu re.
2. Do ni me aoibhneas jonnad feign
is gairdeachas gu mor:
Do tainmse sinnim moladh binn,
O righ is airde gloir.
3. Tra pfilleadar mo naimhdeann garg,
sann romhad sgriostar iad.
4. 'Stu sheasamh dhamh mo choir, 'smo chuis:
shuigh, is thug comhthrom uait.
5. D'imdhearguigh thu na cinnidh borb,
do sgriosfadh leat na daoi:
An ainm do chuir tu as gu glan
o linn gu linn a chaoich.
6. O namh! chuaidh crioch ar sgriosadh nois:
leat chlaoidheadh baillte treun,
An jomradh is a ngcuimhne sud
ghlan theirig iad leo feign.
7. Achd mairfidh Dia gu siorraidh suas,
rinn cathair deas chum breath.
8. 'Is breathnuighidh an sa^ghal gu ceart,
is sluagh le coir fa leath.
9. Mar dhaingneach bidhidh Dia na mseart
don ti ata fa leon:
A ntriobloid 'stearmunn dileas e
re saicsinn neach fuidh bhron.
10. Gach neach da bfuil air tainmse fios
ni dochas diot gu buan:
Oir lion ata ga tiarraidh, Dhe,
nior threig tu iad gu glan.
11. Ceol molaidh sinnibh suas do Dhia,
a nSiodhoin 'ta na thamh;
Is aithrisibh a measg a ntsluaigh
deigh-ghniomhartha a laimh.
12. Tra ni se rannsachadh ar fuil,
cuimhn' orra ni se feign;
Cho dearmaid glaodh an ainnis thruaigh
a shiobhlas erom la pein.
13. Foir orm a Dhe, is toir fanear
mo thriobloid thog luchd mfhuadh:
Os tu ata gam' thogbhail suas
o dhoirsibh bais gu lua.
14. A mpurtaibh inghean Shioin ghloin
gu foillsighionn do chlu:
Is ni me aoibhneas chiond an tslaint
gu grasoil dheonuidh thu.
15. Thuit sios na cinnidh ann fa ndig
do thoehail siad do chach:
Sa nlion a dfholaigh iad a gcein
'ta ngcosa feign a nsas
16. So-aithindh Dia thaoibh breath do ni
tra theid an daoi fa bheinn.
Sa nobair sin ojr glacfar e
do rinn a lamhann feign.
17. Theid luchd an uile a thilleadh uainn
gu doimhne ifrinn gheir:
Theid leo na fineachan gu cruinn
leig Dia a cuimhn' gu leir.
18. An tainnis truagh cho dreid a Dhe,
an dearmaid ort a chaoich,
Air dochas cheairt an duine bhochd
gu brath ni fhaicear claoj.
19. A Thighearn' eirigh 'sna leig buaidh
le neach dhan dual a mbas
Breith thugfar air na cinneachaibh
a tfhiaghnais ann 'sgach cas.
20. Grad chuirfear eagal orra, Dhe,
is faitchios adhbhal, leat;
'Sgu naithnigh geintilidh jad feign
do bheith na ndaoine meat.
SALM X.
CREUD as far sheasmhas fada uam
Jehobha dhearrsgnuidh threun?
An aimsireadh ar ntriobloid mhoir.
creud as sa nfholigh feign?
2. Ta droch-dhuin ann na ardan borb
ag diobhargadh na mbochd;
Achd glacfar jad 'sna hinnleachdaibh
do dhealbhadar chum lochd.
3. Ta ndroch-dhuin' deanamh raith is uaill
an mian a chroidhe feign;
An duine sauntach molaidh se
Dia ge do ghabh dhe grain.
4. An droch-dhuin' aig fior-ardan gru aigh
cho njarr se Dia na ngras
Ni bsuil na chroidh gach uair air Dhia
na smuainte glan ag fhas.
5. A shligh 'ta doilghiosach do ghna
ni msaic do bhreith, aig aird':
Re fanoid air a naimhdibh fos
feididh a phluic began chaird'.
6. Do labhair se 'na chroidhe feign
gu fior cho ghluaisfear me:
A neigin no a nanshocair
cho bhi me feign a chaoich.
7. 'Sro lan do mhollachadh, a bheul,
do chealgoireachd 'sdo gho:
'Ta tubaisd' is gna dhiomhaineas
fuidh theangaisean gach lo.
8. A ndiomhaireachd na ngc^ chann beag
'ta se na shuigh began fhios:
Ag feathamh ar an neimhchiontach
da mhurt' an uaigineas:
Ta shuile ar a ncaogadh fos
re beachdughadh ar bochd.
9. Mar leoghan luighionn se a nceilg
na gharadh, ar ti lochd.
A mplaid na luigh ata do ghna
a mbochd gu glacthar leis:
Na deoridh tairngidh se 'na lion,
is glacfaidh iad le threis.
10. Crubaidh is cromaidh se gu lar
chum dho nach moithiodh neach:
Chum leis a laochraibh fos gu dtuit
a mbochd bhios gabhail seach.
11. A dubhairt se na chroidhe feign,
Sud dhearmaid Dia began cheist,
Is dfholuigh se a ghnuis agceinn,
ni mfaic e so a mfeast.
12. Dhia eirigh, tog do lamh an aird':
na dearmaid deoraidh truagh.
13. An duine dona creud fa ndeun
dimeas air Dhia na nsluagh?
A dubhairt se na chroidh ris feign,
cunndas nach jarradh tu.
14. Sud chunnaic ^hu os leir dot shuil
gach annhleas is gach tnu:
Gu comain thabhairt seach led' laimh
dfhag ainnis ort e feign:
Os tu is oide dhilleachdann
grad fhuasgail air na fheidhm.
15. Gairdein an drochdhuin' is an daoi
leon agus bris a Dhe,
is rannsigh match a aingidheachd
gu nuig nach fuighear e.
16. Ta Dia na righ gu suthain ann,
thuit cinnidh as a their.
17. Mian na ndaoin' umhla chual tu, Dhe;
croidh deas gheibh uait gu fior:
Is bheir tu air do chluas gu neisd:
18. Bheir ceart do dhiobrachann,
'Sdo dhaoine brute, fear on uir
eun fhoirneart los nach dean.
SALM XI.
MO dhochas cuiream ann a nDia
ereud e fa nabradh sibh
Re manam, los mo chur ar gheilt
Teich as mar eun d'ar sliabh?
2. Feuch, chuir na haingidh bogh ar ladh,
soighde ar sreing do ghleus,
Sa ndorch' thoirt urchair ar an ti
'ta ceart na chroidh 'sna bheus.
3. Ma theid na bunachair ar dhi,
Creud ni an duine naomh?
4. Ta Dia 'na theampul naoimh do ghna,
'ta cathair Dhe ar neamh:
Se sgrudfas daoin' le famhra shul,
o chi a shuil gach ni.
5. Dia rannsighidh na fireinidh:
fuadh leis luchd uilc a chaoich:
Is lion bheir sbeis do ragaireachd
is faudh la anam feign.
6. Air dhaoinibh drochmhein dortidh Dia
rib, paintearan is pein,
Garbh. dhoinionn, pronnasc, teine garg:
Sud cuibhrionn luchd drochbheart.
7. Dia comhthrom, 's inmhuin leis a choir;
'ta ghnuis ar dhaoinibh ceart.
SALM XII:
NOis cuidigh linn a Dhia na ngr^s
oir deagh-dhuin' ni bfuil ann:
Na daoine fireanach measg chaich.
re fhaghail taid to ghann.
2. Ar dhiomhaineas re 'ngcomharsnach
taid teachd le miodal beil;
Le croidhe dubailt lan do cheilg
sior-labhraidh siad le cheil.
3. Na beilidh chleachdas gabhann tla
bhios leam is leat began cheart,
An teangca bhruidhneach, ardanach,
glan-sgathaidh Dia na mfeart.
4. Do radh, Buaidh bheir sin orra match
ler 'dteangaidh feign gu beachd:
'S leinn feign ar beilidh, cia an Triath
oirn ga bfuil uachdranachd?
5. Bhridh foirneart ar na deoraidh truagh
is osnaidh dhaoine bochd,
Nois eirghim feign (radh Dia) da dhion
on droing do bhagras lochd.
6. Is fiorghlan briathra Dhe began cheist.
mar airgiod 'taid gu leir.
Do leaghadh, ghlanadh fos fa sheacht
le tein' a nsuacan cre.
7. Ni tu a ngcoimheid uil' a Dhe
on gheineilsi a chaoich:
Imchidh luchd uilc gach taobh gu dan
tra thogfar prascan daoi.
SALM XIII.
CIA fhada dhearmadar me leat,
a Dhia an ann gu brath?
Cia fhad do fholaigheas do ghnuis
gu coimheach uam gach tra?
2. An gcomharligh re manam, me,
'smo chroidh re bron, gach la?
Cia fhad do thogfar tharam suas
mo namhaid mar ata?
3. Nois toir sanear, is eisde riom,
a Thighearna mo Dhia.
Soilsigh mo shuil, 'snach coidil me
trom-chodla bhais gu dian.
4. Deagal gu nabair m'eascar treun
Chuaidh agum air anois;
'Smo naimhde guinneach gu biodh ait
a nuair a dhaomfar meis.
5. Achd dhearnas bun dot' throcair, Dhe,
ad' shlanaigh bidhidh ait.
6. Is sinnim dhuit, a Thriath, fachuis
an phailteas fuair me uait.
SALM XIV.
DO radh an tamadan 'na chroidh,
Ni bfuil Dia idir ann:
Taid truaillidh, is gniomh ghraineoil rinn,
re maith ni bfuil a haon.
2. An Tighearn' damhric se o neamh
ar chlann na ndaoin' gu dian
A fheuchain, tuigseach an raibh neach,
no fear a dhiarradh Dia.
3. Do chlaonadar gu taobh arfad,
to shalach uil', is breun:
Neach ni bfuil ann, ag deanamh maith,
ni bfuil ge beag, a haon.
4. Ciall nach bfuil aig luchd uilc gu leir?
ta 'githadh suas do ghna
Mo phobul mar an aran blast,
'snach gairid air an Triath?
5. Andsin do ghabh siad eagal mor
chiond Dia bhi measg na nsaoi.
6. Na chomhairl' nairigh sibh a mbochd,
os tearmunn Dia dho chaoich.
7. A Sioin tiocfadh slaint' Israil,
biodh Jacob aoibhneach as,
A phobul tra bheir Dia o bhruid
ni Israil gairdeachas.
SALM XV.
CIa fhanas ann do phailuinn, Dhe?
ad thulach naomh ni tamh?
2. Fear ghluaiseas leat gu trebhdhireach,
'sni jonnracas le laimh:
Neach labhras firinn fos o chroidh,
3. Began ithim radh ma bheul
Nach dean ein lochd da chomharsnach,

Nach do ghabh ceannach: fear marsin

SALM XVI:
DHia coimhead me, oir jonnad 'ta
mo dhochas feign gach la
2. O manam, dubhairt tu re Dia,
is tu mo Thriath do ghna:
Cho rig mo mhaitheas ort, a Dhe;
3. Achd do na naomhuibh bhos,
Daoin' oirdheiric a mbsuil mo thlachd,
muil' aoibhncas is mo chlos.
4. Mor-mheuduighear a ndoilghios doibh
a dheibhrigheas gu lua
Ar lorg ein neach nach bfuil na Dhia,

Deoch-iobairt sola-bhios na measg

Cho ghabh me chaoich a mbhilidh ghloin

5. Cuibhrionn mo chup is moighreachd Dia:
'stu sheasmhas dhamh mo chrann.
6. An aitibh aoibhneach thuit mo lion
's leam oighreachd bhreagh nach gann*

'Ta mairne fos an am na haoich

Bhridh gu bfull se aig mo lamh dhea^

Ni msheoil fos comhnuidh fhoistincac^

'S ni leigionn tu dod' sheircin naomh

SALM XVII.
EISD feign a Thighearn' ris a choir,
toir fos fancar mo ghlaodh,
Is cluinn an urnaidh thig amach
o bheul began ghaoid began gho.
2. Mo bhreath o tfhiaghnais thigeadh match;
led' shuilibh feuch ar ceart.
3. A dfhiosruigh tu me ann 'sa noich
sgruduigh mo chroidh gu beachd.
Me rannsuigh Dia, 'sni fuair dhamh maoin;
oir romham chuir me feign
Nach deanam briseadh claon ar bith,
no peacadh bao le 'mbheil.
4. Adtaic re oibribh dhaoine fos
do riaghlughadh fa seach,
Le guth do bheil chum me me feign
o jul an dimhilteach.
5. Cum m'iomachd ar do shlighibh suas,
nach sleamhnuigh uam mo cheim.
6. O gheibh me eisdeachd uait, a Dhe,
do ghairmeas ort am' fheim:
Do chluas dom' ionnsaidh crom anuas,
gabh re mo ghearan feign.
7. Taisbein do chaomh-ghras iongantach,
Dhia, theasraigeas gu treun:
Is le do dheaslaimh shaoras fos
an drong don dochas thu
Da ngcoimheid, is dan teisriginn
on dream a dheirgheas riu.
8. Fuidh sgail do sgesa foligh me,
gleth me mar chloich na sul,
9. On droch-dhuin' ta ga mchlaoi, mo namb
gam' chuartughadh am' iul.
10. Na nsaill ataid ar druite suas,
caint' ardanach na mbeil,
11. Jom-jathadar 'nar cemna sin,
chrom suil gu lar le cheil.
12. Mar leoghan gionnach togarach
chum cobhartigh do ghna,
Mar leoghan og a ndiomhaireachd
ag luigh a mplaid ata.
13. Dhia eirigh, is gabh roimh mo namh
leag sios gu talamh e:
An droch-dhuin' ta na chloidheamh dhuit,
a Dhe, saor manam uaidh.
14. O dhaoinibh 'ta mar lamh dhuit fo s,
o dhaoinibh saoghalta lan,
Ga bfuil a ngcuibhrionn, is a ncuid
'san bheathaidh so amhain
Da bfuil tu tabhairt lan a mbronn
as tulidh dhiomhair feign:
Lan sliochd ataid, is fagsuidh iad
fuighleach a ncuid da ngcloinn.
15. Achd meis a chean, chi me do ghnuis
a msireantachd began cheist
Ar mosgladh dhamh lan-lionthar me
led' chosmhalachd a mfeast.
SALM XVIII.
DIA 's inmhuin leam, se Dia mo threis
2. Mo charraic e gu ceart,
Mo dhaingneach is mo shlanaigheoir;
mo Thighearn' is mo neart.
An ti a ngcuiream dochas fos,
mo thargaid is mo sgia,
Is adharc slanaigh dhamh e feign,
mo thurait ard se Dia.
3. Nois gaiream ar an Tighearna Dia,
ionmholta 'ta gu mor:
Marsin o meascairdibh gu leir
mo shaoradh ni gu lor.
4. Chuir tuilteach dhrochdhaoin' eagal orm,
guin-eug chuaidh iomam feign;
5. Pein ifrionn, agus eangach bais
do choinnigh me gu tren.
6. Am' eigin ghoir me air an Triath,
air Dhia do ebhadh me,
Is as a theampul chual mo ghuth,
na fhiaghnais thainig i,
Mo scread na eisdeachd rainig suas.
7. Chrath talamh, chriothnuigh e;
Ghluais iochtar cnoctha, chrath gach sliabh
bhridh corrigh ort a Dhe.
8. Chuaidh deattach as a shron a match,
loisg teine as a bheul:
Do lasadh eibhle loisgeach leis
tra choinnigh siad a cheil.
9. Lub se na neamha, thainig nuas,
bheith dorchadas fuidh chos.
10. Ar cherub mharcuigh, dhitealuigh
ar sgia na gaoi a bhos.
11. Duibh-dhorchadas mar dhiomhaireachd
do chuir se uime feign;
Budh phubuil uime uisgeadh dorch'
is neulla tiugh na nspeur.
12. Roimh Dhia a neulta tiugh do chuaidh,
is clocha-meallain cruaidh:
Chuaidh cabhla loisgeach match gu sior
o ndealradh bhi na ghruaidh.
13. 'S na speuraibh rinn se tairneanach:
leig Dia a ghuth amach,
Thig cloch-sneacht fos on ti is aird',
le eibhlibh teth fa seach.
14. A shoighde leig se feign amach,
is sgaoil se iad arfad;
Do theilg tein-aidheir orra nuas,
is dfhuaduigh iad gu grad.
15. Grinneal na nuisgeadh chonncas ris,
iochtar an domhain nochd:
Le ossag analach od' shroin.
's led' spreigeadh chiond ar lochd.
16. Chuir nuas, ghlac se, is tharraing me
o uisgibh iomarcach.
17. O meascar threin, is o luchd mfhuadh,
to laidir orm gach neach.
18. Tra ruaig fiad orm a nlo mo theinn:
budh throstan damh mo righ.
19. Da ionad ^hairsinn ^hng me suas,
ghabh tlachd dhiom, shaor se me.
20. Reir mionnracas, is gloine lamh
dhiol Dia gu pailt, maith riom.
21. Om' Dhia gu haingidh chean nior chlaon,
sligh Dhe oir choimhdeadh leam.
22. Uil'-bhreathamhnas bheith roimh mo shuil,
a sdatuim ni chinr tiam.
23. Budh trebhdhireach na shiaghnais me:
sheachain mo lochd gach am.
24. Do rinn a nTighearn' uime sin
mo chuitiughadh, gu caoin,
Reir mionnracas is gloine lamh
an amhrng a shul feign.
25. Don' duine jochdmhoir, jochdmhur t^^*
direach don' trebhdhireach.
26. Glan thu don' duine ghlan, is doirmh
don' duine dhoirmh fa seach.
27. Oir saoraidh tu an sluagh fa theinn:
achd sealladh ard bheir nuas.
28. Soilsidh mo Dhia mo dhorchadas*
'smo choinneal lasaidh suas.
29. Do bhris me buidhionn each led' neart:
tree m Dhia leim balla cas.
30. Sligh' Dhia 'ta ceart, 'sa fhocal glan,
sgia e don' dhearbfas as.
31. Oir cia 'sDia achd Jehobha ann'
cia 'scarraig ann achd e?
32. Se Dia a phaisgeas me le neart,
is ni mo shlighe re.
33. Mo chos rinn lua may ^hosaibh scigh,
chuir me air m'airdibh riamh.
34. Bogh' stalinn bhris mo ghairdeanna,
se sheol gu cath mo lamh.
35. Do thug tu sgia do shlainte dhamh,
do dheaslamh chum me suas,
Do shuairceas caomh thug orm gu pailt,
gu hinmhe mhoir gu dfhas.
36. Mo chemna rinn tu fairsinn sum,
mo chos cho sleamhouigh i.
37. Lean me no namh, rug air gach neach,
sul thillcas uadha, do chluoi.
38. Began cho^ias eirigh lot me iad:
do thuit siad fuidh mo chois.
39. Le neart chum cath do chrios tu me:
na dheirigh riom, do choisg.
40. Ar muineal thug tu dhamh mo namh:
luchd mfhuadh gu sgriosfuinn iad.
41. Ghlaodh siad, 'sda m^uasgladh cho raibh neach
re Dia, 'sni fhreagair se.
42. Andsin mar dhuisleach dol le gaol
gu mion do phronn me iad:
Do theilg me iad amach aris
mar chlabar ar a ntsraid.
43. O chonfadh phobuil shaor tu me,
rinn ceann na mfineach dhiom:
Sluagh fos nach bai^hnidh dhamhsa riamh
nid seirbhis dhamh, do chiom?
44. Comhlua sa chluintear iomradh orm,
dhamh geillfidear began stad:
Ni coigridh dhamh iad feign ar ghne
do isliughadh arsad.
45. Glan-tuitidh as, is teirigidh,
iarmad na nallmhurrach,
Ag teachd le huamhun as a ncuas
'so ngaradh diomhair, match.
46. Ta Dia beo, gu ma beannuight' c,
mo charraic se began cheist:
Is gu raibh Dia mo shlainte feign
ar ardaghadh a mfeast.
47. Se Dia ni dioghla ar mo shon,
'sa mpobal chuireas fum.
48. Se fhuasglas o mo naimhdibh me,
'so dhruing a dheirgheas riom:
Dhia, togaidh tu me os a ngciond,
thug saor on ragair me.
49. Bhridh sud, measg chi^^idh bheir me clu,
is molfam tainm la chaoich.
50. Se Dia bheir fuasgladh mor da righ:
is gras da ungaighth' feign,
Do Dhaibhi, iodhoin, is da shliochd
gu siorraidh mar a gcedn'.
SALM XIX.
GLoir Dhe, na neamha dfhoillsigh dhuinn
'sna speura, gniomh a lamh.
2. Ta la toirt sgeul do la; is aoich
toirt tuigs' do dhoich began tamh.
3. En chaint' no uirchioll ni bfuil ann
a nguth uadha sud nach cual;
4. An riaghail, feadh gach tir chuaidh match,
'sa mbriathar gu crich a ntsaoghail.
Buan-phailuinn chuir se ionnt' don' ghrein
thig match o sheomar dhil
5. Mar dheagh-fhear bainns' le rogha scaid,
'smar ghaisgeach, ait chum rith.

o theas na greine shios.

ag iompoidh anam daoin':
Is cinnteach teastas De, 'sis fior,
's ni glic an tsimlidh bao.
8. Ta sdatuidh fos a nTighearna ceart,
'se fhagbhas croidh gu hait:
Ta aitheanta De to ghlan gu leir,
bheir radharc don tsul nach faic.

Fior agus comhthromach arfad
a bhreathamhnas ata.
10. Is mo, 's ioniarraidh iad no ntor,
moran dheagh-oir gu sior:
Is milse iad no mil dom' bhlas,
'sna shilios nuas on chior.
11. Na cheand sin fos fuair toglach feign
deagh rabhadh nadh gach tra;
Is ann na ngcoimheid curamach
mor-thuarasdal ata:
12. Cia thuigeas chean a sheachrain feign?
glan o lochd dhiomhair me.
13. Gum ^oglach feign o pheacaidh dan*
a nuachdar orm na bid:
Andsin bim saor on pheacadh mhoir,
'so chionfa iomadach:
Atshiaghnais biaidh me gu fior
ceart agus trebhdhireach.
14. O Dhia, mfhearsaoridh, is mo neart,
na briathra 'ta a mbheil
'Sna smuainte bheachduigheas mo chroidh
biodh taitneach riot le cheil.
SALM XX.
GU neisdeadh Dia riot, lo do theinn,
Dia Jacob deanadh leat.
2. O theampul naoimh gud' chuidiughadh,
a Sioin tugadh neart.
3. Biodh cuimhn' ar tuile ofrail aig,
loisg-iobairt gabhadh uait.
4. Do chomhairl' coimhlionadh arfad

an ainm ar nDia do ni
Ar bratighean do thogbhail suas,
Dia dheonach runn do chroidh.
6. Nois 'sfiosrach me gur choimhead Dia

7. Ta cuid ni bun do charbuid catha,

Achd ainm Jehobha, 's Dia dhuinn feign

8. Do isliughadh na daoin' is thuit;
achd deirigh sin is sheas.
9. Dhia foir, is eisdeadh linn an righ,
tra ni sin gearan ris.
SALM XXI.
AN righ ni aoibhneas, Dhe, ad neart
ad' shlainte bithidh ait.
2. Do thugfas mian a chroidhe dho',
'sgach neith do iarr se uait.
3. Oir beannachadh na maitheas moir
gu much do thugfas do,
Is chuir tu coroin oir ma cheann,
don or is glo^^, gach lo.
4. Buan-bheatha djarr se ort. is fuair,
Fuair aimsir chian gu brath.
5. Chuir onoir air is mordhalachd;
's mor uaill ad shlainte, ghna.
6. Lan-bheannuight dhearnas e a mfeast,
to aoibhneach fos led' ghnuis.
7. Oir earbfaidh 'nrigh a Dia is aird;
tree throcair air, cho ghluais.
8. Do lamh bheir t'uile naimhde match,
gheibh do lamh dheas luchd fuadh.
9. Do ni tu iad mar naiamhann loisgth'
an aimsir tfheirg gu lua.
Na chorridh sluigidh Dia iad sios,
is loisgidh tein' iad suas.
10. An toradh sgriosaidh tu on tir,
's an siol o dhaoin' anuas.
11. Oir olc a taghaidh chumadh leo,
beart aimhleasach do dhealbh.
Feall ghrann do bhrath a chur a ngniomh
nach dfheud cur leis gu dearbh.
12 Led' shoighdibh gleusd ar sreing, re ngruaidh
bheir orra dol ar ais.
13. Ad' neart by ard a Dhe, 'sle clu
sior-chanaidh sin do threis.
SALM XXII.
MO Dhia, mo Dhia, creud me far threig:
is tfhurtachd nam a gceinn.
Na briathra goirt dom' bhuiridh ard
creud fa nach cluinn thu feign?
2. Sa nlo do ghlaodhas, O mo Dhia,
achd eisdeachd uait ni suair:
Do thog mo scread riot ann sa naoich,
a mthosd ni bfuileas uair.
3. Achd naomh 'ta Dia, a dhaitigheas
aros chlu Israeil,
4. Ar sinnsir rinn diot bun do ghna,
is shaor tu iad le cheil.
5. Do ghlaodh siad riot, is shaoradh iad:
dhearb riot, 'sni fuair a nclaoi.
Achd mis, ni duine me, achd cnuimh,
grain daoin' is tair a ntsluaigh.
7. Cuis crathadh cinn, is casadh craois,
lion chi me, fanoid ni,
8. Ag radh, Do rinn se bun a Dia,
gu bfuasgladh e na dhi:
Nois deanadh se a theisrigin
o ghabh se tlachd da dhoigh.
9. Achd 'stu an ti bhuain me amach
o bhroinn mo mhathar fa dheoigh:
Sann uait do ghabh me dochas fos
ar chich, is me am' naoidh.
10. Do thilgeadh ortsa me on bhroinn;
on bholg, mo Dhia, 'sa chaoich.
11. Fad uam na by, os dlu dhamh teinn*
fearsaoraidh ni bfuil ann.
12. Do chuartuigh moran tarbha me:
tairbh laidir Bhashan dhan.
13. Is orm a dfhosgil siad a ngcraos,
mar leoghain gionnach geur.
14. Do dhoirteadh mis amach mar uisg
mo chnamhann sgaint' gu leir:
Mo chtoidh am' chuim an taobh a stigh
ar leaghadh 'ta mar cheir.
15. Ar triomachadh mar phota creadh
mo neart ata da reir:
Mo theanga lean i re mo ghiall;
gu huir bhais thug tu me.
16. Oir chuartuigh madraidh garg me nois,
bhuail iomam moran daoi:
Mor-chuideachd los mo dhruideadh suas
lot siad mo chos 'smo lamh.
17. Mo chnamban feudfam aireamh fos,
'taid dearcadh orm began tamh.
18. Mo thruscan eattora do roinn,
croinn chuir siad ar mo bhrat.
19. Na by uam fada, Dhia mo neart,
grad fuigheam cabhar uait.
20. On chloidheamh manam saor, a Dhe,
maon-ghradh o neart a choin.
21. O adharcaibh bhuabhail, bheul an leoghn
do chual tu me o shoin.
22. Dom' bhrathairibh cuiream tainm a ngeill:
'sa neireachd molfam thu:
23. Shiol Jacoib, 'sa luchd eagail De
gloir tabhraibh dho, is clu:
A iarmad Israeil arfad,
biodh oraibh eagal De
24. Oir grain nior ghabh do fhear fa leon
a dhrip nior mhi-mheas e:
Ni mo do fholigh uaidh a ghnuis,
achd chual tra ghlaodh se ris.
25. San tionoil mhoir do mholfam thu;
mo mhoide iocfam nois,
A nlathair a luchd cagail feign.
26. Is ithidh daoine ciuin,
Gheibh iad an sath: lion dhiarras Dia
sior-mholfaid e le runn:
Bhur croidhe bidhidh beo a mfcast.
27. Gach iomal tir ni cuimhn,
Tillidh gach fine sluagh re Dia
is sleachdaidh dhuit gach aon.
28. An righeachd, os le Dia arfad,
se 's uachdran ar gach sluagh,
29. Josaidh slogh reamhra uil' a ntsaoghail,
is onoir bheirid uadha:
Gach ti theid sios don uir 's don uaigh
na fhiaghnais cromaidh dho,
Cho dteid le neach a anam feign
ni 's faid a chonbhail beo.
30. Thig sliochd, do dheanamh seirbhis do;
mheasfar do Dhia mar liun.
Innsid a cheart do dhroing re teachd,
'sgu 'beisean so do rinn.
SALM XXIII.
DIA feign is e is buachail dhamh,
cho bhi me ann a ndi.
2. Bheir se gu luigh me sios gu re
a ngcluanaibh glass le since.
Ata se ga mo threorughadh
re taobh na nuisgeadh mall
3. Ag aiseag manam dhamh ar ais
do chum nach dteid a chall:
Se Idiuras me 'sna slighthibh coir
ar sgath a ainm feign.
4. Da ngluaisfinn tree ghleann dorch' a bhais,
tree dhubhar mar a gceudn,
En olc ni heagal leam theachd orm;
oir 'ta thu, Dhe, far leam,
O chum do lorg 'sdo shlait me suas,
do lean mo mheisneach riom.
5. I^ ^^hair mo naimhdeann dheasuigh thu
board romham feign nach gann:
Mo chup chuir thairis: 's tu a Dhe,
chuir oladh ar mo cheann.
6. Achd leanaidh maith is trocair riom
ar fad mo lo began cheist:
Is comhnaidhim an aros De
feadh dhamh by beo, 'sa mfeast.
SALM XXIV.
SLE Dia an talamh, 'sna bfuil ann:
an domhan, is gach ti.
2. A bunchar leag se ar a chuan;
's ar aibhnibh shocruigh i.
3. Cia fear theid suas gu ^ulach De?
sheasmhas 'na ionad naomh?
4. Fear lamhann glan, is croidh began chaidh',
'snior thog a anam riamh,
Re diombaineas no beairt began sta,
mionn iganach nior lugh.
5. Se beannachd gheibh on Triath, is ceart
o Dhia a shlainte dlu.
6. So geineoil Jacoib dhiarras e,
do ghnuis, Dhe, mar is coir.
7. A gheataidh, togaibh suas bhur geinn,
'sa dhoirseadh, siorraidh mor:
Do chum gu dtigeadh righ na gloir
a steach le buaigh is rath.
8. Cia 'sRi na gloir? Dia neartmhur tr^n,
Dia cumhachdach a ngcath.

10. Cia he so 'srigh na gloir atann
Jehobha mor na nsloigh;

SALM XXV.
DHia togbham manam riotsa sua^.
2. Bun diot, mo Dhia, do ni;
Na buaghuigheadh mo namhaid orm,
'sna leig chum naire me.
3. Is na leig neach fuidh mhasladh ghrann
bhios feathamh ort do ghna;
Achd naire gu raibh ar an dream
ni lochd began chuis gu brath.
4. Nois foilsigh dhamh do shlighea, Dhe;

5. Me treoruigh ann a tfhirinn ghloin,
is teagaisg me a chaoich:
Oir 'stu is Tighearn' ann gu fior,
is Dia mo shlaint' do ghna
Sann ort ata me feathamh fos

6. Dhia cuimhnigh dhuinn do throcair caomh,
's do chaoimhneas lan do ghradh;
An allud fuair sin, is agcian

7. Na cuimhnigh peacadh m'oige dhamh,
no m'easaontas gach re,
A reir do throcair cuimhnigh me
ar sgath do ghrasa, Dhe,
8. Is maith sis direach Dia na ndul:
is ar an adhbhar od,
Do dheanann se na peacaidh thruagh

9. Na daoine seimh is treorulghidh
a mbreathamhnas gu ceart:
'Sna daoine mine teagaisgidh
na shlighe Dia na mfeart.
10. Siad cemana a nTighearna Dia
trocair is firinn buan
Don druing a chonbhas cumhnant ris
'snach caill a theastas glan.
11. Logh, Dhe, mo lochd ar sgatha tainm,
oir ta e mor gach lo
12. Cia fear dan' eagal Dia? do ni
rogha sligh' a theagusg dho.
13. A nseasgaireachd ni anam tamh:
's le shliochd an talamh feign.
14. Runn-diamhra De 'ta leo arfad
dan eagal e gach aon:
Is feuchaidh dhoibh a chumhnant naomh.
15. Mo shuil re Dia gu sior:
Se spionas dhamh mo chosa leont'
nios as an rib gu fior.
16. Till chugam is dean trocair orm;
ta 'm aonar, is a nteinn.
17 Ta cradh mo chroidh ag dol a mead
O fuasguil me om' phein.
18. Dhia feuch ar manshocair, 'smo shaothair,
'smo pheacaidh logh gu leir.
19. Mo naimhde lionmhar toir fanear
fuadh nimhneach thug dhamh feign.
20. Dhia coimheid manam, furtigh orm:
na leig fuidh naire me,
Mo dhochas uile leagfas ort
arson gur tu mo righ.
21. Me dionadh diongmhaltas is coir:
is me ag feitheamh ort.
22. Dhia, fuasguil ar chlainn Israeil

SALM XXVI.
DHia, tabhair breith gu cinnteach orm
do ghluais am' ionnracas:
Chuir me mo dhochas ann sa nTriath:
cho sleamhnuigh me gu cas.
2. Dhe, ceasnuigh agus fidir me;
feuch mairne is mo chroidh.
3. Do dheagh-ghean roimh mo shuil ata:
a tfhirinn dhimigh me.
4. Le daoinibh diomhaineach nior shuigh;
le cealgoiraibh ni chuaidh.
5. Budh fhuadh leam coimhthional luchd uilc,
cha suigh me leis na daoi.
6. Nighfim an neimh-chiontas mo lamh:
is taltoir cuartuigh me.
7. Gu 'ninsinn le fonn bhuidheachais
do mhirbhuilieadh, mo righ.
8. Gna-aite tonoir 'sinmhuin leam,
is comhnuidh aruis De.
9. Na cruinnigh manam le luchd uilc,
no daoinibh fuileach geur.
10. Drong ga bfuil dobhlas mor na nglaic:
lan briba an lamh dheas.
11. Achd gluaisim feign am' neimhchiontas:
le trocair saorsa meis.
12. Na seasamh 'ta mo chos gu beachd
an aite comhnurt re:
Is ann 'sgach coimhthional ni me
do bheannughadh' a Dhe.
SALM XXVII.
Se Dia mo sholas is mo shlaint',
Cia neach is eagal leam?
Se Diasa, neart mo bheathaidh fos:
cia chuireas faitchios fum?
2. Drochdhaoin' mo naimhde, meascairdeadh
tra thainig orm gu bras,
Gu gionnach dithadh mfheola suas,
fuair tuisleadh, thuit gu cas.
3. Sluagh naimhdeoil ge do theisdeadh me,
ni heagal le mo chroidh:
Da neirgheadh cogadh 'madhaidh fos
as so is cinnteach me:
4. Aon ni do jarr me feign ar Dhia,
gu minic jarram e.
Do bhi a mchomhnuigh feadh mo la
gu hait a naros De:
Gu bfaicfinn maise, De, 'sa thlachd,
'sna theampul dfhaghail sgeul.
5. Oir folaighidh na phubuil me
an am na hairc, gach eal:
A ndiomhaireachd a phailuinn fos
do ni se mfholach feign,
Mo shocrughadh do ni faraon
ar carraig dhaingion thren.
6. Osciond mo naimhde 'ta fam chuairt
nois togfar suas mo cheann.
Bheir me ca phubuil, jocfam fos
glan-jobairt aoibhnis ann.
Fonn-molaidh sinnidh me do Dhia.
7. Eisd riom tra ghlaodhas me;
A Dhe, dean trocair orm san am,
is freagair me, mo righ.
8 Tra dubhra is, Jarraidh m'aghaidh re,
do fhreagair dhult mo chroidh,
Se t'aghaidh shoillier lan do ghras,
a Dhe do dhiarras me.
9. Na cuir uait toglach feign a mfeirg,
na foligh uam do ghnuis:
Budh tu mo chongnamh, Dhia mo shlaint',
na treig me nois a mchuis.
10. Tra dhiobras m'athar, me, 'smo mhathar,
me togfaidh tus', a Dhe.
11. Do shligh dhamh treagaisg, treoruigh me
om' namh, a ncasan re.
12. Gu toil mhi iochdmhur meascairdeadh
na tabhair thairis me:
Oir fiaghnals bhreugach dheirigh riom,
dream bhrucas nimh a chaoich.
13. Mo mhe ^^each reachadh nil' ar gcul
mun' ge^ ^inn feign gu cinnt,
Gu bfaicfinn ^aitheas De, 'sa ghras
a ntir na mbeo gach linn.
14. Le foighid fan re Dia na ndul,
glac chugad meisheach mor,
Is neartuighidh do chroidhe dhuit:
fan fos re Dia na glor.
SALM XXVIII.
A Dhia mo charraig, cabham riot,
fad uam ad thosd na by
Deagal mar dhaoin' theid sios don uaigh
mar sin gur cosmhuil me.
2. Eisd re guth mathchoinnidh, a Dhe,
tra ghlaodhas riot am' chas;
Gu diomhaireachd do theampul naoimh
tra thogbham lamhann suas.
3. Le luchd an uilc sna heugcorach
na tarraing me gu brath,
Le ngcomharsan a labhras since,
achd olc na ngcroidh' ata,
4. A reir an oibridh tabhair dhoibh,
'sa ndithchioll ghabhuidh ghoirt;
Is cuitigh riu droch-ghniomh an lamb,
amhluidh mar thoill siad ort.
5. Chiond oibridh De nach tug fancar,
no idir gniomh a lamh:
Cha dean se iad a thogbhail suas,
achd sgriosaidh sios began tamb.
6. Arson guth machoinnigh gu deisd,
mor-bheannuight gu raibh Dia.
7. Dhearb ris mo chroidh, is chuidigh e,
se Dia mo neart, 'smo sgia:
Bhridh sin, mo chroidh ata to ait,
'sle m'oran molfaim e.
8. Se Dia neart slanaigh ungtha feign,
se Dia an neart gach re.
9. Coimheid do phobal nois a Dhe,
is beannuigh toighreachd feign;
Sior riaghluigh agus beathaigh iad,
tog iad a mfeast gach aon.
SALM XXIX.
A Laochraidh laidir, tabhraidh seach
do Thighearna na mfeart.
Don' Tighearn' tugaibh seach, radh me,
gloir, urram agus neart.
2. An ghloir is cubhaidh thoirt da ainm
sin tugaibh seach do Dhia;
A nmais a naomhthachd, teach a ghloir,
grad sleachdaidh sios do nTriath.
3. Ta guth Dhe ar na huisgeacha:
Dia glormhar tairnein ni
Is ar na huisgibh lionmhar mor
ata an Triath na shuigh.
4. Lan mordhalachd guth De ata,
to chumhachdach faraon.

ag briosg^dh ar gach rod,
Sliabh Lebanoin is Sirion
mar bhuabhal meargant og.
^. Sgoiltidh guth Dhe na dealanaigh.

Is dirbhtheach Chadeis mar agcedn
se Dia a chrathas e.
^. Do bheir guth Dhia ar aidhibh allt'

Is ann na theampul naomhtha feign

Ard ghloir is cumhachd Dhe a ngceill

^0. 'Ta cathair Dhe shios ar an tuil:

^1. Bheir neart da phobal; is le since

SALM XXX.
DHia airdghim thu, oir thogbhais me:

SALM XXXI.
DHIA cuiream dochas-jonnad feign
fuidh nair' na leig me chaoich:
O dhoghruinn is o dhaoirse cruaidh
ad cheartais saorsa me.
2. Do chluas dom jonnsaidh aom anuas,
grad furtigh orm, a righ:
Mo charraig laidir bise dhamh,
tigh tearmunn, dhionas me.
3. Oir stu is carraic dhileas damh,

Bhridh sin, Dhia sdiuir is treoruigh me

4. On lion a d'fholigh jad dhamh, Dhe,

Arson gur tu amhain an ti

5. Nois tiomnam suas mo spiorad bochd

Bhi manam ann a nteinn, a Dhe,
is bhi tu fiosrach air.
8. Ni dhearnadh leat mo dhruideadh suas

An aite fairsinn shocruigh thu
mo chosa dhamh gu deas.
9. Dean trocair orm, a Dhia, anois,
oir 'taim a ntriobloid mhoir.
Mo shuile, manam, is mo bhru.
shearg iad le bron 'sle deoir.

m'aimsir le osnadh, chaoich.
Mo neart me threig, do bhridh mo lochd,

11. Budh adhbhar thalcais me began cheist
