15. Atataoi beannuighte o Dhia
rinn neamh is lar atann.
16. Neamh, is na flaitheasa, 'sl'e Dia:
fuair talmhan, clann na ndaoin'.
17. Lion chuaidh gu tamh, cha mhol iad Dia,
ni mo na mairbh faraon.
18. Achd buidheachas is beannachadh
bheir sin do Dhia gu brath,
O so amach gu marthanach.
Molfaibh an triath do ghna.
SALM CXVI.
DIA 'sionmhuin leam, do bhridh gu gcual
mo 'ghuth 'smo ghearan fos.
2. Do ghairfim air re mbheo, fachuis.
gur aom se riom a chluas.

Do chailgeadh me le dhealgnaibh geur,

4. Ghoir me annsin air ainme Dhe:
Saor manam, guidhim ort.

Sar-choimhdidh Dia an tsimlidh truagh,

am dheithfi^ labhair meis.

13. Cailis na saoirse glacaidh me,

14. Lathair a phobuil uile' nois

15. 'S to ridhmheach bas a naoimh' aig Dia.

Do shearbhont, mac do bhanoglaigh:
mo gheimhleadh fhuasgladh leat.
17. Dhuit jocfam jobairt bhuidheachais,
gairfim ar ainme Dhe.
18. Mo mhoideann diolfam nois don' Triath

19 A ngcuirtibh mhuirneach theach mo Dhia,
O thus' Jarusaleam,
'Ta deas na suigh' ad lar a stigh.
O molfaibh Dia, gach dream.
SALM CXVII.
A Righeachda an tsaoghail gu ler
nois tiocfaidh steach le ceol:
Gach pobal molfadh Dia, 'sgach sluagh,
se chruthaigh na bfuil beo.
2. Oir so-chroidheach dhuinn e gu mor,
so chaidridh fos ata:
A fhirinn mairfidh tree bhioth sior.
Molfaibh gach ti, bhur Dia.
SALM CXVIII.
O Beiridh buidheachas do Dhia,
oir maith ata se feign:
Fachuis gu bfuil a mhacantus
ag maireachdainn agcein.
2. Nois abradh Israeil gu bfuil
a ghrasa maithanach.
3. Tigh Aaroin naoimh, gu bfuil faraon
a throcair caoin, gu brath.
4. Nois abradh dreim dan eagall Dia,
iochd gu bfuil aig a mfeast.
5. Am amhghar ghair me ar an Triath,
Dia shreagair me began cheist,
An aite fairsinn chuir se me.
6. Ta Dia ag seasamh leam,
Ni heagail leam, fa neart na ndaoin',
gach aon da neirgheadh riom.
7. Ta Dia ag seasamh ar mo chrann
le meudsa chuidigh leam:
Mo tunn do chi me uime sin
ar dhaoin' an miorunn riom.
8. Sfearr dochas chur a nDia na ngras
no 'nduine 'ta fan ghrein.
9. Sfearr Dia do ghabhail mar chultact
no prionnsa mora tren.
10. S griosfam gach drong do chuartuigh me
an ainm Dhe na nsloigh.
11. Do jadh is theisdeadar fam chuairt:
trid Dhia, achd gheibh a nclaoi.
12. Mar bheicheadh thiomchiolluigh siad me,
achd chasgadh iad ari^s
Mar theine droighean: oir an ainm
mo Dhia, iad sgatham sios.
13. Sath nimhncach thugfais chugam feign,
is thulgfadh meisi leat
Do los gu dtuitfinn sios fa d'chois,
achd chuidigh Dia me uait.
14. Se adhbhar m'oran Dia, 'smo neart,
mo shlanaigh nois a chaoich.
15. Glor ghairdeach^s, is fuaim na slaint'
'ta 'mpailuinn na nsaoi:
Rinn deaslamh Dhe gu tabhachdach
16. Thog deaslamh Dhe an aird:
Gu cruathalach rinn deaslamh De,
17. Ni mfuigheam bas began chaird:
Achd mairfidh, cuiream fos a ngceill
gniomhartha Dhe 'sgach cas.
18. 'S goirt smachduigh Dia me: achd nach tug
tur thairis me gu bas.
19. Dhamh fosglaibh port na corach suas
is gabhaidh me a steach
A thabhairt moladh dhligheach uam
do Dhia 'ta os gach neach:
20. So geat ar nDia, theid orra steach
na daoine trebhdhireach.
21. Dhia, molfam thu, oir chual tu me:
mo shlaint' is tu gu beachd.
22. An chloch do dhiult na clochaireadh
cloch-bhraigh' na huillinn si,
23. Sud obair Dhe, 'ta jongantach
re amharc air, gu fior.
24. So la do dhearnadh dhuinn le Dia,
biam to shuilbhir ann,
25. ^oirdhion nois, guidhim ort a Dhe,
cuir chugainn sonas buan.
26. Beannuight' an neach do thig nar measg
an ainm a nTighearna mhoir:
Do bheannuigh sin sibh o chian
a haros Dhia na gloir.
27. Se Dia an Tighearna, thug dhuinn
solas is soirbheas sen;
An jobairt ceanguilibh le teud
re adhaircibh 'naltoir feign.
28. Is tu mo Dhia, sior-mholfam thu;
fior-arduighim mo Dhia.
29. Dho tugaibh buidheachas, ^^a maith;
a throcair mairfidh 'ngcian.
SALM CXIX.
ALEPH.
IS beannuight' na bsuil glan 'san tsligh,
lion shiobhlas a nlagh Dhe.
2. Beannuight' na daoin', a theastas ni,
'sle nuil-chroidh dhiarras e.
3. Eugcoir ni dheunaid sud, no lochd:
gluaisfid na echlidh' ghlan.
4. Do aithin thu gu gcoimhdeadh sin
do reachd gu toigheach buan.
5. Dan sdiuirtheadh mjul ar cheim do lagh
O b'aoibhin damh an ni.
6. Tuil' aitheanta tra bheir me fanear,
orm, cho chuir masladh, chaoich.
7. Bheir me le chroidh to threbhdhireach
gu meanmnach moladh dhuit
Ar foghlaim dhamh do d' chomhthrom dheas
an bhreathamhnas, gu hait.
8. Do statuideadh gu gcoimhead me
'se runn mo chroidh gach re:
O Dhia, na dibir me gu heug,
gu tur na treig me feign.
BETH
9. Creud ghlanas jul don' oganach?
reir tfhocal stiuradh i.
10. Na leig od' reachd ar seachran me,
dhjarr thu le m'uile chroidh.
11. A taghaidh los nach dean me lochd,
cheil tfhocal ann mo chroidh.
12. Dhia teagaisg dhamh do statuid dhlu,
os beannuight thu, a chaoich.
13. Le m' bheilidh chuir me uil' a ngceill
deagh-bhreathamhnas do bheil.
14. Budh ait a njul do theastais me
mar ann sgach neith, fan ghrein.
15. Air thorduigh beachduighidh mo chroidh,
air hechlidh 'smor mo speis.
16. Ad' statuid 'ta mo shaimh, 'smo thoil:
'tfhocal om' chuimhn' cho dteid.
GIMEL.
17. Re toglach dean gu toirbheartach:
a Thighearna na mfeart,
Gu mbiam beo marsin trid ghras
ag coimheid tfhocal cheart.
18. Fosguil mo shuileann dhamh, 'sgu bfaic
od^ lagh beairt jongnadh, me.
19. 'Sa chruinne 'taim am' choigreach bochd:
na ceil uam taitheanta, chaoich.
20. Is manam sgaradh 'ta, a ngeall
air do bhreath cheart gach am.
21. Daoin' uaibhreach, mollaight', chronuigh thu
chuaidh siar ar thaitheantaibh glan.
22. Tog mimheas uam, is masladh g^ur:
do theastas choimheid me.
23. Na ro-dhaoin' is na prionnsa mor
labhair am' adhaidh, Dhe;
Achd smuaintigh toglach feign gu beachd
air do dheagh reachd do ghna.
24. Do theastais fos a siad mo thlachd,
is luchd mo chomhairle, 'ta.
DALETH.
25. 'Ta manam leanmhuin ris an uir:
reir tfhocal beothaigh me.
26. M'iul chuir me 'ngceill, is chual thu me^
do statuidh, teagaisg i.
27. Toir tujgse dhamh ar sligh' do reachd,
gach aithne chuireas uait:
Air hoibridh jongnadh annamh ris
sior-labhraidh me gach ait'.
28, 'Ta manam leaghadh sios le bron:
reir tfhocal neartuigh me.
29. Fiar-sligh' na breige seachain uam,
is deonuidh dhamh a Dhe,
Do lagh gu gradhach caonmharthach
dom'sheoladh ann sgach beairt.
30. Fior-sligh' na firinn thaghadh leam:
chuir romham do bhreith cheart.
31. Lean me re d' theastais dlu: a Dhe
na cuir gu naire me.
32. Theid me ar jul do lagh am' rith,
tra leathnuighis mo chroidh.
HE.
33. Dhia teagaisg 'sligh' do statuidh dhamh,
gu deire coimhdim i.
34 Toir tuigse dhamh, is ni do thoil,
ni me le m'uile chroidh.
35. Toir orm by trial a nceim do lagh:
oir maoibhneas ann ata.
36. Aom chum do theastais feign mo chroidh,
's nior hann chum sainnt gu brath.
37. O dhearcadh ar an diomhaineas
mo shuileann till a Dhe:
Is beoaigh gu hard-mheanmnach
ad' shlighe dbireach, me.
38. Tfhocal, dot' shearbhont, socrach dean,
oir gheill do teagail mis.
39. Till uam' mhio-ghloir, chuir eagal orm:
oir 'smaith do bhreathamhnas.
40. Feuch lean me feign gu curamach
an diaghaidh t'orduigh cheart:
O beoaigh me a tfhireantachd
Dhia threbhdireach na mfeart.
VAU.
41. Tiocsadh do throcair orm, a Dhe,
'sdo shlaint' reir tshocal cheart:
42. Freagradh bheir me marsin don' fhear
rinn talcals orm gu fiat.
Oir earbfuidh me re tfhocal naoimh.
43. Na toir om' 'bheil anois
Focal na firinn, Dhe, gu tur:
o dhearb red' bhreathamhnais.
44. Is amhluidh coimhidfim do lagh
gu bioth-bhuan ar gach achd.
45. Is siobhlaidh me gu saor-lamhach,
oir dhjarr me riamh do reachd.
46. Ma d'thcastais labhraidh me gu dan
abfiaghnais righthe tren,
Eun mhasladh dheth, no naire throm
cho ghabthar sin leam feign:
47. Do taitheanta, 'stoigh leam, gabham tlachd.
48. Togfam mo lamhann suas
Chum taitheanta 'sinmhuin leam: is ni
ad' statuidh smuainte fos.
TZAIN.
49. Do toglach cuimhnigh tfhocal fhior,
air dhearnais dochas damh.
50. Aon-mheisneach dhamh am' dhoghruinn gheir
gur bheoaigh me, le d' ghuth.
51. 'Sro sgigeoil luchd a mhordhail,
gidheagh od' lagh nior chlaon.
52. Do cheartais chimhnigh me o chian:
ghlae meisneach me faraon.
53. Fachuis luchd uilc, do threig do lagh
ghlac uamhun me gu trom.
54. Do lagh an aros m'oilithridh
ba o^ainn binne leam.
55. Tainm chuimhnigh me, a Dhe, san aoich,
is choimhead me do reachd.
56. Fuair me an solassa, do bhridh
tiartas, rinn me gu beachd.
CHETH.
57. Mo chuibhrionn, 'stu a Dhe, radh mi^
tfhocal gu gcoimhlion me.
58. Do fhuraileas le m'uile chroidh'
do ghean 'sdo ghnuis gach re.
Reir tfhocail deunsa trocair orm.
59. Tra smuaintigh me ar mjul.
Mo chosa, chum do theastais ghlain
do pfill me, Dhia na ndul.
60. Began fhuireach, dheibhrigh me gu lua
ar coimheud thaitheanta caoin.
61. Shlad buidhionn dhrochdoaoin' me: gidheadh
nior leig do lagh a cuimhn'.
62. Grad eirghidh me fa mheadhon aoich
do thabhairt buidheachas duit:
Chiond gu bfuil breathamhnas to cheart
a Dhe, ga dheanamh leat.
63. 'Sme seiseadh dhaoin 'dar heagal thu,
'sna choimhideas do lagh.
64. Ta ngcruinne, Dhe, jom-lan dod' ghras
do statuid teagaisg dhamh.
TETH.
65. Re toglach 'smaith mar fuaradh tu,
reir tfhocail feign, a Dhe.
66. Deagh-chiall, is eagna teagaisg dhamh,
oir chreid me taitheanta feign.
67. Sul ghuasadh me, ar seachran chuaidh,
achd tfhocal coimheud nois.
68. Is maith tu Dhe, 'sre deanamh maith,
ad statuidh teaguisg meis.
69. Gu meabhlach, luchd an ardan borb
do dhealbh am' aghaidh, breug;
Achd torduighthe, Dhe, coimhdidh me
le m'uile chroidh', gu heug.
70. An gcroidh' comhreamhar 'ta re saill:
ad' lagh achd 'ta mo thlachd.
71. Smaith dhamhsa gu do chraigheadh me.
'smo phianadh fuair gach achd:
A gcoinne oileamhain thoirt dhamh
ad' statuid chinnteach bhuan.
72. Sfearr lagh do bheil dhamh no gach nail
don or 'sdon airgiod gblan.
IOD.
73. Toir ciall chum taitheanta thuigsinn, damh,
do lamh me rinn is ghleus.
74. Tra chi luchd theagail mis, bid ait:
o^dhearb re tfhocal feign.
75 Dhe, 'sfiosrach me do bhreath bhi ceart:
's gur bhuail a mfirinn, me.
76. Do shuarcais tugadh comhfhurtachd
reir tshocal, dhamh a Dhe.
77. Caomh-throcair, Dhe, gu suigheam uait,
marsin gu by me beo:
Os tlachd is toileach-inntin damh
do reachd 'sdo lagh gach lo.
78. Air dhaoine diomsach gu raibh nair',
gam ruaigeadh 'ta gu beachd,
Gu fiat, began adhbhar chathuigh orm:
achd smuaintighim ad reachd.
79. Riom tilleadh lion dar heagal thu,
is ghabh air theasdais fios.
80. Mo chroidh biodh foirfe ann do lagh,
is ni ngabh naite meis.
CAPH.
^1. Leon manam bochd a nlorg do shlaint':
earbfam ad' bhriathar gu hait.
^2. Chion tfhocail lag mo shul, ag radh
Ca huair gheibh solas uait?
^3. Mar bholg sa ndeattach chinn me nois,
do lagh cho dearmaid me.
^4. Ca li^on laith toglaoich, is ca mead
an aimsir do gheibh se?
Ca huair do chuireas tu a ngniomh
ceart-bhreath air luchd mo thoir.
^5. Chlaoich sluic dhamh daoine ainmeineach
nach seol an sligh' ar choir.
^6 T'uil' aitheanta 'sfireanach, a Dhe:
foileanmhuin rinn gach ti,
Gu heugcorach chaith dochair orm;
O cuidigh leam, a righ!
^7. Beag nach do chlaoi siad me san tsaoghail
achd torduighthe nror threig.
^8. A reir do chaoimhneas beoaigh me,
'sdo theastas ni, gu heug.
LAM^D.
^9. Bith-dhaingnionn tfhocal, Dhe, ar neamh
90. Ta tfhirinn do gach linn:
An talamh shocruigh thu gu caomh,
is seasmhaidh suas gu cinnt.
^1. Reir thorduigh maithrionn 'taid a njugh,
oir searbhont dhuit gach ni.
^2. Mun' bhi do lagh na sholas dhamh;
a mdhrip reachfuinn ar dni^
^3. Torduigh cho dearmaid me a chaoich:
Oir bheoaighis me leo.
94. 'Sleat feign me, saor me; oir do dhjarr
torduighthe me, gach lo.
95. Dsheith orm na daoi dom sgriosadh as:
dod' theastais toigh bheir me.
96. Fiorchiond gach foirfeachd chunnaic mis:
's foirleathan taithcanta, Dhe.
MEM.
97. Ca hionmhuin leam do lagh: a Dhe,
's mo smuain air, feadh on lo.
98. Trid thaitheantaibh 's glioca me no m'namh
oir leam ataid rem' bheo.
99. Is tuigsigh me no m'oideadh muint':
oir ghabh air theastais, beachd.
100. Sharuigh mo chiall na seanoireadh:
o choimhead me do reachd.
101. Mo chosann o gach aon droch sligh'
do chonbhadh leam ar ais:
Do chum gu bfed me tfhocal fior
choimhead gu siorraidh nois.
102. Nior ghluais me, Dhe, od' bhreathamhnais
'stu theaguisg me le ceill.
103. Ca miochar 'ta do chaint' dom' bhlas?
's milse no mil dom' bheil.
104. Trid torduighte roi-chneasd, a Dhe,
deagh eagna gheibh mo chroidh:
Sligh mheangach, mheabhlach uime sin
is fuadh leam feign a chaoich.
NUN.
105. Is coindeal, tfhocal naomh, dom' chos,
is solas glan dom' cheim.
106. Do mhionnaigh, is coimhlionfaidh me
do cheart-bhreath coimhdfear leam.
107 Ar m'eigniughadh ataim gu mor:
reir tfhocal beoaigh me.
108. Gabh nam saor-ofraileadh mo bheil
muin damh do cheart, a Dhe?
109. Am' laimh 'ta manam leon do ghna:
'sni dhearmaid me do lagh.
110. Sas-gabhala leag dhamh na daoi:
do reachd njor threig, gidheadh.
111. Do theastais ghabh mar oighreachd bhuan
siad aoibhneas glan mo chroidh'.
112. Gu d'statuidh chojmhed, da^om mo chroidh
do ghna', 'sgu nuig a chrich.
SAMECH
113. Is fuadh leam smuainte diomhaineach:
do lagh achd 'sionmhuin leam.
114. 'Stu m'ionad folaghaidh, 'smo Sgia:
do tfhocal bun do nim.
115. Luchd drochbheart, rachaibh fada uam:
oir lagh mo Dhia ni me.
116. Reir tfhocail dean mo chonbhail suas,
a mbeathaidh, is gu by:
Nar naire dhamh mo mhuinighinn:
117. Cum suas, is tearnuidh, me:
Is bheir me feart, do d'statuid cheart
Dhia, ann sgach beairt, a chaoich,
118. Stu shaltair air luchd seachran, Dhe,
od' riaghail chuaidh, gu leir:
Oir faille, briseadh geallaidh fos
fe sud is ciard dhoibh feign.
119. Mar sgim do chuirfeas uait na daoi:
sud sath mo ghaoil do d'reachd.
120. Do teagail, criothnughadh 'ta mfheoil,
ghabh fiamh me roimh do smachd.
GNAIIN.
121. Do dhearnadh comhthrom leam, is ceart^
na fag faoi shladoibh me.
122. Air thoglach by a ndils' ar nihaith:
na creachadh me na dao^.
123. A ndiaidh do shlainte charthanaigh
mo shuile failneadh 'ta,
Arson na mbriathra dileas fos
do tfhireantachd, do ghna.
124. Dean Dhe, do toglach reir do ghra^s,
do statuid teaguisg dhamh.
125. Do shearbhont 'sme, toir tuigse dhamh,
's gu n'aithnigh me do lagh.
126. Is mithidh dhuit neith chur a ngniomh,
do lagh chuir iad o bhuil.
127. Siad taitheanta 's andsa leam no 'ntor,
an tor is glaine neal.
128. Tuil' orduighthe, Dhe uime sin
adtaice ris gach ni
Iad measfaidh me do bhi to cheart:
gach fiar-sligh 's fuadh lem' chroidh.
PE.
129. Do theasdais, jongantach ataid;
coimhedfidh manam iad.
130. Ceud tosuigheadh do bhriathra naoimh
ar solas chuir an mead:
An tsimlidh tais gheibh tuigse uaidh,
is an mao-oglach mea^.
131. Dfhosguil mo bheul, leig osnadh me
a ngeall ar thaitheanta ceart.
132. Orm amhairc, is dean trocair, orm,
ceart mar is bes leat sein
A dheanamh ar do dhaoinibh gaoil
thug cion dot' ainm, gu leir.
133. Ceannas aig eugcoir na biodh orm:
a tfhocal sdiur mo chem.
134. Saor me o fhoirrneart bhibhionach:
sin taitheanta nithear leam.
135. Air thoglach dealruigheadh do ghnuis
do statuid teagaisg dhamh.
136. Shruith aibhne uisg' anuas o mshuil
chiond nach dean iad do lagh.
TSADDE.
137. O Dhia, ata tu fireantach*
is trebhdhireach do bhreith.
138. Do theastais dhorduigh thu, taid ceart,
ro-dhileas 'taid gu seth.
139. Chaith m'eud me baileach: bhridh mo namh
gur threig do bhriathra re.
140. Is fior-ghlan tfhocal: uime sin
is toigh le toglach e.
141. Is lag ataim, 'sbeag speis 'ta dhiom
achd taitheanta cho loig uam.
142. Ta tfhireantachd to mharthanach:
do lagh se nshirinn ghlan.
143. Rug inghreim orm, is amhluadh mor
Achd taitheanta siad mo thlachd
144. Ceartas do theastais siorraidh' ta,
bim beo, le ciall do reachd.
KOPH.
145. DHIA eisd re scread mo chroidh 'smo chleibh
do statuid coimhdfidh me,
146. Do ghlaodhas riot, saor me: 'sannsin
do theastais feign do ni.
147. Leig osnadh me roimh' nsgaranaigh
rinn bun do d' bhriathar anois.
148. Sul thionsgain fairthe aoich ar teachd
a tfhocal smuaintigh mis.
149. Do reir do chairdeas gradhach feign
eisd re mo ghuth, a Dhe;
Do reir do bhreathamhnas 'ta ceart
ath-dhuisg led' neart sa me.
150. Dhruid sluagh riom, lean beairt aimhleasach,
is fad ghabh iad od' reachd.
151. Tuil' aitheanta siad an fhirinn ghlan:
's dlu dhuinn thu, Dhe, gu beachd.
152. Adtaic red theasdais, baithnidh dhamh
o chian gur tu do rinn,
Gur tu fos shocruigh iad gu deas
chum by a mfeast far linn.
RESH.
153. Toir m'anshocair fanear, 'smi saor?
do lagh cho dearmaid chaoich.
154. Foir orm, is tagair dhamh mo chuis:
reir tfhocal beoaigh me.
155. Do shlainte 'sfada ghabh on daoi
nach djarr do statuid mhaith.
156. 'Smor, pailt, do throcair eaomh, a Dhe,
me beothaigh reir do bhreath.
157. Mo naimhde, luchd mo dhiomhargadh
is laidir, lionmhur jad:
Achd mis nior dhaom od' theastais fhior,
scho chlaon gu fior chum beud.
158. Budh tru^gh leam luchd na heugcorach
tra thug me iad fanear:
Fachuis nach dearnadh tfhocal ceart
a choimhead leo, mar dhiarr.
159. Feuch mar is toigh leam thaitheanta, Dhe
me beoaigh reir do ghean.
160. Ta tfhocal fior o thus: gach aon
bhreath cheart lea^, 'ta a gcian.
SHIN.
161. Lean prionnsa oram began chion-fath;
is d'eignigh me le neart.
Achd mis, budh sgathach bhi mo chroidh,
caglach roimh tfhocal cheart.
162. Ma tfhocal 's aoibhneach me, mur neach
suair cobhartach to mhor.
163. Is suath 's is graineoil leam an bhreug;
achd 's toigh leam do lagh coir.
164. Seachd nuaire molfam thu gach laoi:
bhridh ceartais naoimh do bhreith'.
165. 'Smor siothchaimh dhaoin' thug gaol dod'lagh:
cuis saobhnais ac' cho bhith.
166. Bhi suil red' shlanaigh agam feign,
is taitheanta rinn faraon.
167. Do theastais, choimhead manam iad:
to ionmhuin leam gach aon.
168. T'uil' orduighthe do coimheud me,
'sdo theastais naomh began cheist:
Oir romhad feign 'ta muile cheim
is m'uile shligh' a mfeast.
TAU.
169. Mo scread a tfhiaghnais thigeadh nios,
gu dlu a Dhe, ort feign:
Reir tfhocail tabhair tuigse dhamh
dod' ghrasa caomh, a Dhe.
170. Fad' chomhair tiocfadh mathchoinnidh*
saor me mar gheallas tu.
171. Ar faghail ciall do statuidh uait
nochdfuidh mo bheul do chlu.
172. Ma tfhocal ni mo theangca sgeul,
t'uil' aitheanta, 'sceartas iad.
173. Do lamh, gu deanadh congnamh leam
oir torduigh thagh me riamh.
174. B'fhad leam an dail bhi 'd shlanaidh dhuinn,
se m'uile thlachd, do lagh.
175. Biodh manam beo, is molfuidh thu:
led' bhreith, beir cobhair dhamh.
176. Mar chaoragh caillt', chuaidh fathban, me
jarr toglach feign gu d' chro.
Oir taitheanta ceart, nior dhearmaid me,
'scho leig a cuimhn', re mbeo.
SALM CXX.
AM'chruaidh-chas ghlaodh me ris an Triath
is chual se me gu lua.
2. Saor manam Dhe, o bheul na breig
'son teangaidh mheangach thla.
3. Creud bheirthear, no creud nithear dhuit,
a theangthaidh mhialldach mhin?
4. Sar-shoighdeann seaiteach laochraidh ghasd',
le eibhlibh eiteal feign.
5. Mairg meis ata comhfhad ar chuairt
a Mesec allmhurrach:
Am' thamh 'ta fos am' puiblibh dhoirbh
don' Chedar Araipeach.
6. Is fad rinn manam caidreadh ris
an neach do fhuathuigh since.
7. Sfear-siothchaimh meis: achd tra ni guth,
an chogaidh taid ar ti.
SALM. CXXI.
RE sliabhthaibh toguidh me mo shul
o bfuil mo chabhar teachd.
2. Ta mfhurtachd teachd o Dhia na ndul
rinn neamh is lar gu beachd.
3. Cho leig se sgiorradh goirt do d'chois:
tfhear-coimheid pramh cho ghabh.
4. Feuch, air chul-choimhead Israel
an ti ta shuas ar neamh,
Clo codail e, no smeadarnach
cho ghabh, no toirchiom suain.
5. Se Dia 's fear air ort; is sgail
ar do laimh dheis gach uair.
6. Cho ghon an ghrian thu ann sa nlo;
san oidhch fio ghealach fhuar.
7. Ni Dia do choimheud o gach olc:
is dionaidh tanam uadh'.
8. Do dhol amach, 'sdo theachd i steach
a theasaircin ni Dia,
O so a leth is coimhdear, thu,
don' aimsir fhad a gcian.
SALM CXXII.
BUDH ait mo chroidh', tra dubhraid riom,
Tiocfaim chum arois De.
2. Seasmhaidh ar gcos taobh stigh dod' pho^
Jarusalem gu re.
3. Do thogbhadh suas Jarusaleam
mar chathair chruinne, dhlu:
4. Da hionnsaidh theid na treabha suas,
theid treabha De, le clu,
Chum ionad fiaghnais Israeil
thoirt buidheachas do Dhia.
5. Annsud gach cathair bhreathamhnais
taid suighighte gu breagh:
Taid caithrcacha thigh Dhaibhi naoimb.
6. Guidh clos is osadh ghna
Theachd air Jarusalem: mor-rath
thig ar na bheir dhuit gradh.
7. Sioth gu raibh ar do bhallaibh stigh
sonas ad' ghrianan ard.
8. Ar sgath mo bhraithribh, luchd mo phairt
a deirim nois began chaird,
Deagh fhiothchaimh gu raibh agad stigh
9. Arson an tigh' la^n gloir
A nseilbh a nTighearn' ar nDia ata
^arram do mhaith gu mor.
SALM CXXIII.
RIOT togbham suas mo shuil, a Dhe,
ad' chomhnuidh 'ta air neamh.
2. Mar dhearcas sul luchd muinntir, feuch
ar laimh an maighisdireadh.
Mar sul mhnaoi innilt fos re laimh
a ban-mhaighisdir feign:
Marsin ata ar sul re Dia
oirn trocair no gu dean.
3. Dean trocair, Dhe, dean trocair oirn,
luigh athais oirn, le tair;
Is annsath oillteoil fuaramar
do mhiomhodh ghrann, 'sdo nair'.
4. Lionadh ar nanam do mhi-mheas
gu hainmiosarrach,
Le fochaid dhaoine 'ta gu sasd',
'sle raith' na nardanach.
SALM CXXIV.
NOIS feudfaidh Jsrael a radh'
Mun' bhi Dia air ar gcrann:
2. Mun' bhi an Tighearna far linn
tra dhcirigh daoine rinn:
3. Annsin do shluigeadh iad sin beo
an gcorruidh rinn tra las.
4. An tuisg' do bhathadh sin: an sruth
chuaidh thar ar nanam suas.
5. Reachadh na srutha ailghiosach
grad thar ar nanam dhuinn.
6. Beannuight' gu raibh an Tighearna Dia
nach tug da mfiaclaibh sin;
Mar chuibhrionn is mar chobhartach.
7. Do theich ar nanam uadh'
Mar eunlaith do chuaidh as o ghaist'
an eunadoir gu lua:
Bhriseadh an rib, is thearuinn sin.
8. Ar congnamh deas do bhi
An ainm Jehobha^ chruthaigh neamh,
is talamh, leis gach ni.
SALM CXXV.
LION chuireas muinighinn a nDia
mar Shion bid, an tfliabh
Nach feadthar athrughadh a chaoich
achd mairfidh si gach eal.
2. Mar dhiath gach sliabh Iarusalem
is amhluidh chuartuigh Dia
A phobal feign gach taobh le ghras
o so amach a gcian.
3. Oir slat an daoi cho tamh a chaoich
ar gcrann an fhireun choir,
Deagla gu sin a lamh an tsaoi
amach gu heugcoir mhoir.
4. Do dhaoinibh maith, dean maith a Dhe,
's don trebhdireach a ngcroidh.
5. A dtaic re daoinibh theid a taobh
dan slighe fhiar, gach ti
Le luchd an uilc 'sna heugcorach
iad treoruigh' Dia le cheil:
Achd siothchaimh sona, suilbhir, sen
bidhidh ar Israeil.
SALM CXXVI.
BRUID Shiodhoin tra thill Dia air ais
mar dhaoin' a mbruadar sin.
2. Sin lionadh dhuinn ar mbeul le gair'
ar dteangaidh fos bhi binn.
Annsin deir siad measg chinneacha,
gniomh mhordha dhoibh rinn Dia.
3. Cuis mhordhalach rinn air ar son
dfhag ait ar gcroidhea uaidh.
4. Till ris ar braighdeannas, a Dhe,
mar thuil an airde deas.
5. Daoin' shiolchuireas gu dubhach leon
buainidh gu subhach brais.
6. A mfear theid match gu deurach truagh
le rogha siol na bhrat,
Began cheist ag jomchar leis a scuaib
thig ris, gu buaghach ait.
SALM CXXVII.
MUn' tog an Tighearn' suas an tigh
saothair chaillt' a ngniomh ni cach.
Mun' choimheid Dia a mbaile fos
luchd air cho dean sta.
2. Is diomhain daoibh by 'geirigh much,
is anmoch ar bhur gcois,
A dhitheadh aran ghoirt na mpian:
da sheircin bheir se clos.
3. Feuch, gineoil, 's oighreachd iad le Dia:
toradh a bhronn, a fhiach.
4. Mar fhoighde a nlaimh churaidh chruaidh
'ta clann na hoige breagh'.
5. Beannuight' an duine sin ga bfuil
a bholgan lan diobh so:
Cha ghabh siad nair, achd ceannsuighidh
'sa gheat, na naimhde, leo.
SALM CXXVIII.
BEannuight' gach ti da neagal Dia:
do ghluaiseas ann na roid.
2. 'Stu chealaigheas o shaothair do laimh;
do shonas theid a moid.
Is eirghidh leat gach neith gu maith.
3. Mar fhineamhain do bhean
Bhias tarbhach dhuit ma chliach do thigh
slait-olaidh og do chlann,
Ad timichioll do bhuird gu cruinn,
na ntlachd dhuit, is nan' neart.
4. Feuch, sud mar gheibh se beannachadh
da neagal Dia gu ceart.
5. Bheir Dia a Sioin beannachd dhuit,
is maith Jarusalem.
6. Chi tu red' bheo: is sliochd od' chloinn,
le since or Israel.
SALM CXXIX.
ILphian iad me o m'oig' gu tric
nois abradh Israel:
2. Gu minic chathuigh orm o moig
feudfar a radh na sgeul:
Achd buaidh cho tug siad orm amach,
'scho d'eirigh tharam suas.
3. A dh'ar na treabhoich ar mo dhruim,
's fad tharraing iad na clais'.
4. Ta Dia ceart-bhreathach: cuird na ndaoi
ghrad ghearr e as a cheil.
5. Trom-amhluadh orr', is dol ar ais
bheir fuadh do Shioin feign.
6. Biodh siad mar fheur ar mullach teach
do chrionfas sul fa nfhas:
7. Nach lion ochd, aig fear-ceangail scuaib;
don spealadoir, no lamh:
8. Ni mo their daoine ghabhas seach,
Dia thabhairt beannachd dhuibh:
Dhuibh guidhmid soirbheas ann sgach ni
an ainm Dhe, 'ta libh.
SALM CXXX.
A Doimhnibh ghlaodh me riot, a Dhe.
2. Dhia, eisd re guth mo bheil:
O aom do chluas gu ^urachar
re fuaim mo ghearain feign.
3. Da dtugadh tu fanear gach lochd:
O Dhia, cia sheafmhas suas?
4. Achd maitheamhnas 'ta leat, do chum
teagal bheith oirn, 'sgach cas.
5. Ta m'shuil re Dia, dfheith m'anam air;
na shocal m'earbsa 'ta.
6. Nois feathaidh manam ar an Triath,
mo thogra 'smo gu Dia
No togra aig luchd air feign
re sgarthanaigh an la:
'S mo fos, no diaidh na mfairthireadh
ar theachd na maidne, 'ta.
7. Sar-mhuinighinn 'san Tighearna mhoir
nois cuireadh Israel.
Oir trocair saor ata le Dia,
is Saoirse pailt le cheil.
8. Da phobal Israel bheir se
comh-fhuasgladh re, gu grad
O eugcoir is o naimhdeannnas,
o mpeacaidh sos arfad.
SALM CXXXI.
NI bfuil mo chroidhe ammeineach,
nior thog an a^ird, mo shuil:
Ni mo re gnoidhibh mor, no cuis
'ta os mo chiond, bhi m'iul.
2. Gu demhin dhiomchar me mi feign
mar lein'bh diolt on chich:
Gu samhach dfhuirigh manam fos
mar naoidh, 'sa mhathar da dhith.
3. Deagh-dhochas cuireadh Israel
anois a nDia na mfeart
O so amach a saoghal na nsaoghail,
gu suthain mar is ceart.
SALM CXXXII.
DHia cuimhnigh Dalbhidh, 's nile theinn.
2. Mar mhionnaigh se don Triath,
'S mar thug se do Dhia neartmhur moid
do Jacoib 'ta na Dhia.
3. Gu fior fa dhruim mo theach cho tig
ar leapthoidh cho dteid suas:
4. Cho tabhair codla do mo shul,
cha smeid na famhra nuas.
5. Gu nuig a mfuighim alte deas
do Dhia an Tighearna threin,
Deagh ionad comhnuidh nois arson
Dia neartmhur Jacoib feign.
6. Feuch, chual sin uim' aig Ephrata^:
air fonn na coille, fuair.
7. Fior-sleachdaidh sin aig sdol a chois,
'sda phubuil theid gach uair.
8. Dhia eirigh, tarr anios do d' chlos
thu feign, is airc do neart.
9. Do shagarta ar sceadughadh
gu raibh le fireancachd:
Togbhadh do naoimh deagh-iolach ait.
10. Na iompoigh adhaidh uait
(Ar sga do shearbhont. Daibhi naoimh)
and shir do ungadh leat.
11. Do Dhaibhidh mhionnaigh Dia, gu fior,
cho dteid se uaidh a chaoich,
Cail thoradh glan do thig od' chorp
cuirfim ad' chathair righ.
12. Mo chomhcheangal, 'smo theastas cheart
ni meis' a theagasg dhoibh:
Da ngcoimhdeadh sud led' chlainn gu beachd;
an sliochdsa gheibh fadheoigh
Gu suighid air do chathair gu buan.
13. Oir Sion thagh ar nDia:
Ghabh toil dhi, mar a aitreabh feign.
14. Mo shuaimhneas so agcian:
Annso sann ghabhas me gu tamh,
oir 'smian leam i gu beachd.
15. A foireann beannuighim, sa lon:
diol arain gheibh a bochd.
16. A sagairt euduighim le slaint;
bladh aoibhneach bheir a flaith'*
17. Bheir me ar adharc Dhaibhi 'nsud
gu sgeith a blath a match:
Lochran dom' ungtha dhorduigh me.
18. Is euduighidh me fos
Le nair' a naimhdeann: achd air feign
by coroin ur ag fhas:
SALM CXXXIII.
CA maiseach thig e is ca maith
do bhraithribh by le cheil
Na ngcomhnuidh jonand ann na 'ngcroidh',
is aonsgeulach na mbeul?
2. Ta sud mar rogha uinnimeid
dhoirtear ar cheannaibh daoin',
Do shruthlas ar an fheosog sios
ar sheosaig Aaroin feign,
Rith leis, gu leith-imeall a bhrat
tree jonmhar ghreist, aris.
3. Mar dhruichd air Hermon, 'smar an druchd
chuaidh ar sliabh Shioin sios,
Oir sud an ait' a ndorduigh Dia
a bheannachd thabhairt seach,
Is maille ris gach tabhartus,
a bheatha mharthanach.
SALM. CXXXIV.
FFUCH, beannuighibh an Triath arfad
a shearbhonta do Dhia
'Ta seasamh feadh na haoich began stad
an aros ghlan ar nTriath
2. Na naomh-theach togaibh lamh, gu naomh,
is beannuighibh Dia tren.
3. A Siodhoin Dia gu d'bheannughadh
rinn neamh is talamh feign.
SALM CXXXV.
MOlsaibh an Tighearn', molfaidh ainm
O sibhs' a mhuinntir feign.
2. An chuideachd sheasmhas a ntigh De,
a ngcuirtibh De to thren.
3. Molfaibh an Tighearna 'ta maith:
oir 'scroidheoil sud gach lo.
4. Jacob thagh Dia, is Israel
na jonmhas airid dho.
5. Oir 'saithnidh dhamh, Dia, mordha bheith,
'sna Thriath osciond na ndee.
6. Ar neamh 'far talamh rinn na b'aill,
a mfairg', 'sa ndoimhnibh feign.
7. O imeall talmhuin bheir don' cheo
dol suas le teas na grein',
Chuir dealanach arson na mfros,
bheir gaoi as uluidh feign.
8. Neach sgris ceid-ghin na Heighipht as,
na daoin' 'sna hainmhidh fos.
9. Chuir comharth a a-lar do their
O Eighipht, do gach sors':
Air Pharon nochd beairt iongantach,
'sar luchd a theach gu leir.
10. Do sgrios e sios na righeachda mor
is mharbh na righthe treun.
11 Mar Sihon, righ na nAmorach,
is Og righ Bhashain ghast
'S gach righeachd bheanas do Chanaan,
dshuaduigh na finich ast.
12. A nduthaidh thug na oighreachd re
da phobal Israel.
13. Tainm naomhtha mairfidh, Dhe, gu brath,
'sdo chuimhne do gach eal.
14. Oir ceartas bheir an Tighearna Dia
da phobal feign gu cas.
A dtimicheall a shearbhontuidh
gabhaidh se aithreachas.
15. Taid jodhoileadh na ncginneach dall,
don' airgiod is don' or,
Obair do dhealbhadh suas le laimh
na ngclochaireadh 'sna nsaor.
16. Beul aca 'ta, 'scho labhair iad,
began radharc 'ta an suil.
17. Lean cluasa riu, cho chluinn gidheadh,
anail ni bfuil na mbeil.
18. Na dealbhadoire ghleus iad suas
gu cuimir chuaidh riu feign:
Marsin gach ti, bun diobh do ni
na neigin chruaidh, 's na mfeim.
19. Achd beannuigh Dia, theach Israel,
thigh Aaroin, beannuigh Dia.
20. O beannuigh Dia an Tighearna mor,
thigh Lebhi naoimh a gcian:
Dia beannuigh, sibhs' dan eagal e.
21. A Sioin 'fbeannuight Dia
'Ta ngcomhnuidh aig Jarusaleam.
O molsaibh uil' an Triath.
SALM CXXXVI.
Toir gloir do Dhia, oir maith 'ta se:
oir 's marthanach a ghras.
2. O beiridh bhuidhe re Dia na ndee:
oir mairfidh 'throcair suas.
3. Do Thriath na nTighearna toir clu:
oir 's marthanach a ghras.
4. Beairt mhiorbhuildeach do rinn gu dlu
oir mairfidh 'throcair suas.
5. Don' ti le ghliocas chum na nspeur:
oir 's marthanach a ghras.
6. Thar nisgeacha do shin gach tir:
oir manfidh 'throcair suas.
7. Don' ti do rinn gach solas mor:
oir 's marthanach a ghras.
8. An ghrian do riaghlughadh an lo
oir mairfidh 'throcair suas.
9. Gealach is reulta sdiur an aoich:
oir 's marthanach a ghras.
10. Sgris ceid-ghin Eghiphteach gach ti:
oir mairfidh 'throcair suas.
11. Thug Israel match uadh' a gcein:
oir 's marthanach a ghras.
12. Le gairdein sinnt', is lamhaibh tren:
oir mairfidh 'throcair suas.
13. Don' ti rinn da leath don' mhuir ruagh
oir 's marthanach a ghras.
14. Is dhaisig trid a lar an sluagh:
oir mairfidh 'throcair suas.
15. Chrath Pharo uaidh', 'sa fheachd sa chuan
oir 's marthanach a ghras.
16. Threoruigh a dhaoin' tree nfhasach bhuan:
oir mairfidh 'throcair suas.
17. Don ti sgrios rioghruidh cumhachdach:
oir 's marthanach a ghra^s.
18. Is riogha ainmeoil mharbh fa seach:
oir mairfidh 'throcair suas.
19. Mar Sihon righ na nAmorthach:
oir 'smarthanach a ghras.
20. Is Og righ mor na mBashanach:
oir mairfidh 'throcair suas.
21. Is thug an tir na oighreachd ghlan:
oir 's marthanach a ghras.
22. Da shearbhont Israel gu buan:
oir mairfidh 'throcair suas.
23. Neach chuimhnigh nar beig-inmhe sin,
oir 's marthanach a ghras.
24. O'r naimhdibh garg is shuasguil sin:
oir mairfidh 'throcair suas.
25. Don' ti thug beatha do gach duil:
oir 's marthanach a ghras.
26. Do Dhia ar flaitheas tugaibh clu:
oir mairfidh 'throcair suas.
Samhuil oil Meadrachd don tSalm chedna.
DIA gradhach molfaibh nois
A throcair mairfidh ghna.
2. Dho tabhraibh buidheachas
Na Dhia na ndee ata:
Oir 'sdeimhinn linn.
Gu mair' a ghras
Gu cinnteach suas
A^ feadh gach linn.
3. O molfaidh ceann na nTriath
Da bfuil lan-iochd a chaoich,
4. Se feign amhain an neach
Beart jongantach do ni:
Oir 's deimhin linn, etc.
5. Neach flaitheas rinn le ciall.
Ta throcair caomh gach lo
6. Noach talamh ti, o chian
Shin thar an fhairge fos:
Oir 'sdeimhin linn, etc.
7. Don ti rinn solas mor
a ghras oir mairfidh chaoich.
8. An ghrian ni jul don lo
ghna no gu dtuit an aoich:
Oir 's deimhin linn, etc.
9. Gealach, is reulla aoich
Oir 's marthanach a ghras.
10. Don ti le neart do chlaoi
Ceidghin na Heighipht fos:
Oir 's deimhin linn, etc.
11. Is Israel thug as
Buan-ghras oir thug se seach.
12. Le laimh to neartmhuir, dheis,
'Sle gairdein sinnt' amach:
Oir 's deimhin linn, etc.
13. Do sgoilt se a mhuir ruagh.
'S bith-bhuan a throcait saor.
14. Is thug ar Israel truagh
Dol tioram tridh a clar:
Oir 's deimhin linn, etc.
15. Achd Pharo bhaith, 'sa luchd.
A throcair oir is buan.
16. Tree nfhasach chruaidh, is thug
A dhaoine feign gu slan:
Oir 's deimhin linn, etc.
17. Don' ti, chlaoi riogha mor.
A ghras cho chriochnuigh feast.
18. Eachtach, ainmeoil a nglor
Na righthe mharbhadh leis:
Oir 's deimhin linn, etc.
19. Sihon ri Amorach
A ghras oir mairfidh buan,
20. Og calma Bhasanach
Ri foirtill sgris se uainn:
Oir 's deimhinn linn, etc.
21. Thug se an tir a nseilbh,
'Ta 'throcair marthanach.
22. Da Israeil gu dearbh.
Mar oighreachd dhoibh ma nseach:
Oir 's deimhin linn, etc.
23. Neach chuimhnigh oirn nar dteinn:
A ghras cha dteid a cuimhn'.
24. Is shaor o'r naimhdibh sin
Thug fuadh began adhbhar dhuinn':
Oir 's deimhin linn, etc.
25. Neach do gach beo bheir biagh:
A ghras ata a mfeast.
26. A Bhuidh' beiridh do Dhia
Rinn flaitheamhnas gu deas:
Oir 's deimhin linn, etc.
SALM CXXXVII.
RE taobh na naibhne shuigh sin sios
aig Baibilon da bfuil,
Is Sion tan do chuimhnigh sin
do leig sin burail guil:
2. Ar chrannaibh soiligh chroch ar gcruit
an inmheadhon na tir,
3. Annsin drong thug sin leo a mbruid
sheir oran uainn gu fior:
Na daoine dfhasaigh sin gu tur
dhiarr aighear oirn, ag radh',
Aon oran sinnibh dhuinn gu binn
measg orainn Shioin bhreagh.
4. Ciondas thig sin air cheol an Triath
a nduthaidh choimhigh bhoib?
5. Da rachadh tu, Jarusaleam
a mfeast a ndithchuimhn' orm,
Gu dearmaid reachadh mo lamh dheas
ar huile ealadhan ghrinn.
6. Mun' chuimhnigh me Jarusalem
leanadh mo theangc gu cinnt
Re m'chairein is re braigh' mo bheoil;
mun' mheas me feign do chlos
Jarusaileam, cathair theampuil, De
thar m'aoibhneas airidh bhos.
7. Siol Eadhom, cuimhnigh thusa Dhe,
a nlo Jarusalem,
Do radh, Sior-sgriosaibh, sgriosaibh i
ga hiochdar sios, san am.
8. O inighean na Baibioloin
do fhasaighthear gu lom:
Is beannuight neach bheir samhuil duit
mar dhearnais duinn gu trom.
9. Is beannuight e do bheireas uait
do naoidheanna sdo chlann,
Is spadfas iad re clochaibh cruaidh
aig mead an uilc atann.
SALM CXXXVIII.
LE muile ^hroidh' do mholfam thu,
dhuit sinnim lathair na ndec.
2. Fachomhair fos do theampul naoimh,
Dhia, adhram dhuit gu re
Tainm molfaidh me arson do chaoin,
is firinn ghlan do bheil
Oir mhoruigheadh leat tshocal naomh
thar tainm chaoimh gu leir.
3. San lo do ghlaodh me, fhreagair thu,
do manam thugfais neart.
4. Gach righ 'sa chruinne, molfuidh thu
tra chluinnid tfhocal ceart.
5. Is sinnidh iad a nslighe Dhe:
oir onoir Dhe, is mor.
6. Ge hard an Tighearn', bheir e uidh
don' irisil, gu lor:
Achd luchd an ardan fada uaidh
an aithniughadh do ni.
7. Da ngluaisfinn tridh cheart-lar na truaigh
aith-bheoaighidh tu me:
Do lamh is seinfidh tu amach
anadhaidh fearg mo namh,
Is teasraigidh do dheaslamh me
an am mo shaothair, 'smo thamh.
8. Bheir Dia na fhuraileas orm, gu crich:
Dhia, 'smarthanach do ghras,
Na treig, 'sna diobair oibreadh' aill'
led' lamhann dhearnadh suas.
SALM CXXXIX.
O Dhia, do rannsuigh thussa me
fios ghabh tu orm, arfad.
2. Mo shuigh is m'cirghe 'saithnidh dhuit,
tuigidh mo smuain a mfad.
3. Mo cheim 'smo luighe chuartuigh thu,
muil' echlidh 'saithnidh dhuit.
4. Focal ni bfuil am theangaidh Dhe,
nach bfuil gu soillier riot.
5. Romham, 'sa mdhiaidh theisd thu me,
is chuir tu orm do laimh.
6. Bhi nteolassa to jongantach
ar fon mo thuigse riamh:
Ta 'ngliocassa comh-ard, nach feud
me teachd na choinne, dlu.
7. Ca hionad theid od' spioraid me?
c'ait theichfeas me od' shuil?
8. Da riogiuinn flaitheas, 'ta tu ann:
a nmordhalachd 'sa nglor:
Mo leaboidh 'n ifrionn fos da ndean,
'ta 'nsin do chumhachd mhor.
9. Da nglacfuinn sgiatha mhaidin ghil
gu tamh an jomal cua^n:
10. Me threoruigheadh do lamh andsin,
's^o dheaslamh ghlacadh, lua.
11. Da nabrum. Dorchadas gu fior
ni folach orm od' shuil.
An aoich budh doirche umam sein,
bhiodh dhamh na sholas evil.
12. Cha cheil an dorchadas gu fior
achd dealraidh aoich mar la,
An solas is an dorchadas
'taid jonand duit gu brath.
13. Oir m'airneadh shealbhuigheais gu dlu
is mor do chlu, a Dhe.
Chuir folach tharam suas gu deas
a mbroinn mo mhathar feign.
14. Dhia molfam thu, oir dhearnadh me
gu huamhur, jongantach,
Is maith 'ta fios aig manam fos
do ghniomh bheith mi^rbhuilteach.
15. Cho raibh mo shubstaint foluight' ort
tra dhearnadh me a ncleith.
'Sna fonnaibh jochdarach gu gleust
tra ghreiseadh me fa leith.
16. Mo dhealbh na ebeadh chunnaic thu,
'sgach ball dom' chorp, began ghleus
Bhi sgriobht' ad' leabhar, cumtha fos
nuair nach raibh haon ar sgeul*
17. Cia priseoil Dhe, do smuainteadh dhamh?
cia mor an suim 's an luach?
18. Dan airfinn iad, is liugh, gu fior
no gaineimh mhin a chuain:
Arrmosgladh dhamh, ata me leat
a Thighearna do ghna.
19. Gu deimhin marbhaidh tu an daoi
re holc a chaoich, ata:
Grad ghluaisibh ar an adhbhar ud
a dhaoine fuileach uam.
20. Oir labhradar a taghaidh, Dhe,
gu haingidh, is gu dan.
Do naimhde luaigh siad ainm do ghloir
gu diomhaineach na mbeil.
21. Nach fuath leam iad, a Dhia na ngras
gach neach bheir fuath dhuit feign?
Ma dhaoinibh dona, 's doiligh me
a dheirgheas riot gu brais.
22. Is fuadh leam le fuadh nimhneach iad.
meas naimhdeann' orr' bheir mis.
23. Dhia fidir, sgrud mo chroidh: 'sme feuch
gabh colas ar mo smuain.
24. Amhraic mas doiligh, dona miul,
'sme 'fdiur sa ntsligh' bhi-bhuan.
SALM CXL.
ON drochdhuin' saor me, Dhe: is dion
o fhear an fhoirrneart, me.
2. Ta 'gcruinniughadh do ghna chum cath;
is aimhleas dhealbh na ngcroidh.
3. An teangtha scaireach gheuruigh siad
mur bheathar bheimeanach:
Nimh' dhimhilreach nathair-uain ata
fuidh bheilidh, aig gach neach.
4. Dhia dion o laimh 'nfhir aingidh me,
neach eignigheas gu teann.
Ta brath ar m'jomachd is mo cheim
do theilgail bun osceann.
5. Oir dfholuigh luchd an ardan, boinn,
is rib do chuir na bhun;
Re taobh na slighe sgaoil iad lion;
is gaiste ar mo shon.
6. Re Dia a dubhras, Stu mo Thriath,
mo ghearan eisd gu cas.
7. O Dhia an Tighearn', neart mo shlaint',
do dhion mo chiond 'sa chath.
8. Na haontuigh Dhe, re mian na ndaoi,
a chleas na soirbhidh leis,
Deagla gu togfaid ciond an aird
re mortachus a mfeast.
9. Adtaic re ceann luchd jadhadh orm,
aimhleas a mbeilidh feign
Mar thruscan tiocfadh thart gu trom.
10. Le heabhlaibh loisgeach tren,
'Sa teine tilgfeadar, gach ti,
a nslochdaibh doimhne fos,
A ndubh-aigean na huaimh, do chum
nach eirigh iad ni 'smo.
11. Nar chuireadh bunachas san tir
fear bhios re caineadh dhaoin':
Sealgaidh a olc an ragair' feign
da chlaoi, began lamh na thaobh.
12. Is fiosrach me gu seasmhadh Dia
agardas duine leon:
Is conbhaidh coir re daoinibh bochd
ata sa reachd, 'sfa bhron.
13. Began cheist bheir daoine trebhdhireach
do tainmse buidheachas;
Atfhiaghnais, daoine fireanach
do gheibh siad comhnuidh deas.
SALM CXLI.
DO ghlaodhas riot, a Dhia na ngras,
grinnigh dom' jonnsaidh feign,
Is tabhair air do mo ghuth
tra eigheam riot gu tren.
2. A tfhiaghnais reachadh murnaidh suas.
mar spiosra cumhraidh buan.
Biodh togbhail suas mo lamhann fos
mar jobairt-fheasgair ghlan.
3. Luchd air, cuir fachomhair mo bheil,
doirrse mo bheilidh, dion.
4. Na aom chum eun droch ni mo chroidh
mi-ghniomh a chaoich gu dean
Le daoinibh chleachd an eugcoir mhor:
nar itheam da mbiagh blast.
5. Is cairdeas, buill' an duine choir,
is oladh breagh', a smachd,
Cha bhris a achmhasan mo cheann.
na ndteinn, theid urnaidh uam.
6. Tra theilgeadar ar mbritheamhuin,
san sgairnich, bonn tar cheann,
Rem' bhriathraibh eisdidh jad gu hait,
oir taitneach bid gu leir.
7. Sgaoileadh ar cnamhann dhuinn anois
aig beul na huaigh' le cheil,
Mar ghearras is mar sgoilteas neach
a mfiogh ar thalamh teann.
8. Achd riot mo shuile 'taid, a Dhe,
san Tighearn' mearbf' atann:
Na leigsi manam bochd ar dhith.
9. Dion me on eangach ghleust
Do leag luchd uilc, dom' chur a nsas,
is coimheid me on ghaist'.
10. Na droch-dhaoin' tuiteadar gu cas
'sna liontaibh ghleus iad feign,
Feadh dhamhsa teurnodh uadh' arfad,
is jomachd thart gu leir.
SALM CXLII.
DO ghlaodh me le mo ghuth re Dia:
lem' ghuth rinn m'eaccaoin ris.
2. Dhort me mo ghearan roimh' gu goirt;
ar m'ambghar thug me fios.
3. Tria bhi mo spiorad jonnam baitht',
sin b'aithnidh dhuit mo cheim;
San tsligh' ar shiobhlas, shuighigh iad
a ndiamhair, rib dhamh feign.
4. D'amhraic air mo laimh dheis, is fheuch,
'snior ghabhadh duine riom?
Theich uam mo thearmunn: cho raibh neach
chuir manam bochd a nsuim.
5. Da ghlaodh me riot, a Dhe, raidh me
Mo dhidean 'stu a mfeast;
Mo chuibhrionn fos a ntir na mbeo
se Dia gach lo began cheist.
6. OF taim gu craidhteach, crom, a Dhe,
mo screadach eisd anois:
Saor feign me o luchd m'eigniughadh
oir 'streasa iad no mis.
7. A priosun tabhair manam bochd,
is molfar tainmse leam:
Gabhaidh na firenidh fa mchuairt,
oir ni tu sochair riom.
SALM CXLIII.
DOM athchoinnidh toir air', a Dhe,
re m'urnaidh eisd led' chluas;
Is freagair mis a tfhireantachd,
ad' cheartais eisd gu lua.
2. Na himbir breathamhnas gu garg
ar thoglach anbfann feign,
Ni heidir le eun neach ad' lathair
teachd saor amach od' bheinn.
3. Oir, toir air manam lean an namh
bhuail sios mo bheath' gu garbh,
A ndorchadas thug orm by 'mthamh.
mar dhaoin' bhi fada marbh.
4. An meid gu bfuil mo spiorad stigh
ar muchadh jonnam feign:
An taobh a stigh dhamh 'ta mo chroidh
na fhafach mar a gcedn'.
5. Ta 'naimsir o chiond fhad am' chuimhn':
air hoibre ghabh me beachd!
Is smuaintigh ar an tsaothair ghrinn
do lamhann rinn, fa seach.
6. Mo lamhann 'ta me seineadh match
do tionnsaidh feign, a Dhe,
Ta manam ghabhail tart ad' lorg
mar thalamh tioram ^re.
7. Eisd riom gu lua, o's lag mo chroidh',
do ghnuis na foluigh uaim,
Deagal gur cosmhul me re daoin'
theid sios don uamh le gruaim.
8. Cluinfim ma d' mhaitheas caoin gu much
oir bun do dhearnas diot,
Seol dhamh an iul air shiobhlas me
oir togbham manam riot.
9. Saor me, a Dhe, o meascairdibh:
teichim dom' fholach leat.
10. Teagaisg do thoil'se dheanamh, dhamh,
oir 'stu mo Dhia, gach ait:
Is maith do spiorad, treoruigh me
gu ti^r na hionnracas.
11. Sgath tainmse beoaigh me, a Dhe,
is biam meanmnach as.
A triobloid tabhair manam nios
ar sgath do cheartais, Dhe.
12. Sgris naimhdeann manam sios dod' ghras,
oir 'smeisi toglach feign.
SALM CXLIV.
DIA gu ma beannuight e, mo neart,
mo lamhann theagaisg dhamh
Gu cumase is gu eomhlann cruaidh,
'smo mheura chum an chath.
2. Mard-thurait is mfhear-saoraidh deas,
mo dhion, rinn maitheas riom,
Mo sgia, se Dia, mo dhochas buan:
cheannsuigh mo phobal fum.
3. Creud e an duine dhuits' a Dhe,
gu gabhais eolas air?
No mac an duine dhuit, creud e,
gu tugfais e fanear?
4. Is cosmhul e re diomhaineas.
a re, mar sgail theid uainn.
5. Lub Dhe na neamha, tarr anuas,
thig ceo, is bean re beinn.
6. Cuir teinteach uait, iad sgaoil o cheil:
caith soighdeann orr' da nsgrios.
7. Leig nuas do lamh, foir orm, is saor
on tuil, 'so nchoigridh mis.
8. Sud jarmad labhras caint' began bhridh;
lamh chealgach', an lamh dheas.
9. Nua-oran sinnim dhuit, a Dhe,
ar psaltuir bhinn, anois;
Ar adhbhuidh cheolmhar, dheich-teudach
dhuit sinnim, Dhia na ndul,
10. Is e bheir buaigh do rioghruibh tren
is slainte sen, na njul:
Is e ni Daibhidh anacal
on chloidheamh mhillteach bhrais.
11. Saor me, is buain o laimh began jochd
na njarmad coimheach cas.
Da bfuil caint' dhiomhaineach na mbeul,
lamh mhialldach, an lamh dheas.
12. Ar gclanna-mac gu biodh nan oig'
mar gheuga dfhasas brais:
Ar ninghean' mar chloich-uillne snaitht'
ar nos na nlughart mor.
13. Ar gcisdeachadh bhi lan do lon
samhail do nuile stor;
Jondas gu by ar gcaoirigheachd
ag breith na milte uan;
Nar sraidibh fos gu haighearach
deich mile ag teachd uadh',
14. Gu mbi ar daimh gu sultmhar slan,
le fulang saothair na mbraigh':
Began jonnsaidh oirn, no briseadh uainn,
's began ghearan goirt nar sraid.
15. An sluagh dan dual a inmhesi
is beannuight' iad began cheist:
Mas eadh gu hairidh, sona iad
dhan Dia an Tighearn' a mfeast.
SALM CXLV.
TOGBHAM do chlu, mo Dhia, a righ:
tainm beannuighim began tamh.
2. Dhia, guihheam gloir theachd dhuit gach la
sior-mholfam tainm naomh.
3. 'S mor Dia, jonmholta fos gu mor;
doth-rannsuighe ata
A mhordhachd is a ghreaghnachas
aig aird' a ghloir, do ghna.
4. Molfadh gach linn do ghniomh dha cheil,
innsidh ma d' ghaisge threin.
5. Tairngrim ma sgeimh do mhordhalachd,
'sma toibridh annamh feign.
6. Na daoine aithrisidh ma neart
do chuise uamhun ard,
Is uaisle tinmhe os gach ni
sud nochdaidh me began chaird.
7. By iomradh ac' gu pailt 'sgu dlu
air ainm do mhaitheais mhoir?
Is sinneadar gu hait a chlu
bheanus do d' ghniomhaibh coir.
8. Fior ghrasoil, lan do throcair, Dia:
is mall do ghabhas fearg,
Achd 's mor a jochd is acara,
ainmeoil a chaoin gu dearbh'.
9. Chuaidh 'throcair caomh thar uile ghniomh:
achd 'smaith Dia do gach ti.
10. Sar-mholfaidh toibridh thu ar fad,
dhuit beannuighidh do naoimh.
11. Thig siad ar ghloir do righeachd dheas
nid sgeul ma d'neart, gu lor.
12. Do chur a ngceill do chlainn na ndaoin'
ta bhachd do ghniomha mor:
Le neart is buaigh a righeachd ghloin,
'ta maiseach mordhalach.
13. Is righeachd siorraidh, righeachd Dhe,
'ta 'shlaitheas marthanach.
14. Na daoine thuiteas sios gu trom
ni Dia a ngconbhail suas;
An chuideachd bheith gu craiteach crom
'se thogbhas as gach cas.
15. Ta suil gach creatuir dearcadh ort,
biagh bheir thu dhoibh na thra.
16. Ar fosgladh dhuit do la^mh, do gheibh
gach ni 'ta beo an sath.
17. Ta Dia na uile shligh to cheart,
fial, naomh na uile ghniomh.
18. 'S dlu Dia don' mheidsi ghairmeas air:
ghair air a mfirinn, riamh.
19. Ni toil na ndaoin' dan cagail e:
is eisdidh se re nglaodh,
Tra leigeas iad an scread amach
iad fuasgluidh se faraon.
20. Is dionaidh Dia an chuideachd sin
bhias jonumhuin air feign:
Achd daoine dona sgriosfaidh Dia,
luchd uilc, gheibh claoi gu leir.
21. Air chlu an Tighearn' thig mo bheul,
lain-bheannuigbeadh gach neach
'Sgach duil, a ainm naomh le ceol
gu brath o so amach.
SALM CXLVI.
ARd-sinnibh moladh Dhe gu binn.
O manam, mol an Triath.
2. Feadh dhamh bhi 'mbeathaidh molfame,
gloir sinnidh me do Dhia.
Is sinnidh me feadh 'smaithrionn damh,
dom' Dhia, mo mhuinghinn dheas.
3. Na gabhuibh mar chultact dhuibh feign
na prionnsa tren a mfeast,
No mac an duine aig nach bfuil
furtachd ar bith re feim.
4. Theid anail as, theid ri's 'na uir,
ag dol ra dhualghas feign:
Se sud lo chailleas e gu tur
a smuainte ailghiosach.
5. Dan dion Dia Jacob, 's beannuight e,
rinn bun da Dhia gu brath.
6. An neach do chruthuigh neamh is lar,
an fhairg' is na bfuil ann:
A fhocal choimhideas gu ceart,
'sa ghealladh fior, gu buan:
7. Neach chuireas breathamhnas a ngniomh
do dhaoin' ata fuidh leon;
Neach bheir don ocrach teachd a ntir:
fhuasglas na cimigh fos.
8. Ta Dia ag fosgladh sul na ndall:
togbhaidh an leonta crom:
Is inmhuinn leis na daoine ceart
a aitheanta leis nach trom.
9. Is didean Dia don' choigridh chiuin,
's do bhanntrachadh gach eal;
Furtachd na ndilleachdan: achd sligh'
na ndaoi, chur thar a cheil.
10. Sar-riogholuigh an Triath gu buan,
do Dhia s', a Shioin dheas,
Ar feadh gach geineoil bhias ann.
Dia molfaidh leam a mfeast.
SALM CXLVII.
O Beannuighibh do Dhia: o's maith
by sinneadh clu ar Triath;
O's obair thlachdmhur cheadfach e,
's fior-aluinn moladh breagh.
2. O thogbhas Dia Jarusaleam
aris gu maiseach tren;
Is thionoileas na fogarthaidh
dhiobradh o Israel.
3. Se liaighiseas na bfuil brist' na ngcroidh'
an gcreuchdainn cheanglas suas.
4. Dhairmheas na nreulta jomarcach,
dan ainmiughadh gu lua.
5. Is mor ar nTriath, to mhor a threis:
do-thomhais 'ta a chiall.
6. Na daoine ceannsa togaidh Dia:
teilgidh na daoi bun-siar.
7. Sinnibh dar nDia le buidheachais,
le clarsigh sinnibh dho.
8. Le neullaibh chumhduigheas na n'speur,
deagh-fhreasdal gheibh gach beo;
A mfearthuin is an uisge glan
don' talamh dheasuigh se;
Thug ar an fheur gu fas gu hur
air bheanntaibh mordha, re.
9. Se bheir a bhiagh don' ainmhidh seach,
'sdo phreachain og ag gairm.
1 Cha ghabh se tlachd a nspionnadh eich
no 'nlurgna duine ghairbh.
11. Is tlachd leis lion dan eagail e
ni bun da ghras a gcian.
12. Do Dhia, sin O Jarusaileam,
O Shion, mol do Thriath.
13. Oir crainn do gheatuidh neartuigh se:
bheannuigh do chlann gach ti.
14. Le brod an chruithneachd lion se thu:
lan-siothchaimh chuir ad' chrich.
15. Ar dtalmhuin chuir e seam a match,
a fhocal rith gu lua.
16. Mar chluimh do thug se sneachd: is sgaoil
an lia-readh mar an luaith.
17. Leic-eighre chuir mar sbruileach uaidh:
cia sheasmhas roimh a fhuachd?
18. Leig guth amach, is leagh iad ris:
sheid suinnein gaoith a nuas,
Builsgidh na huisgeacha thar board.
19. Fuair Jacob guth a bheil,
A statuidheadh 'sa bhreathamhnas,
thug sin do Israeil.
20. Drong riamh cha raibh fuair amhluidh uaidh:
adtaic re orduigh' cheart
Dream coimheach fos nior dfhairigh iad,
O molfaibh Dia na mfeart.
SALM CXLVIII.
DO Dhia o fhlaitheas deanaibh ceol:
le mor-bhladh molfaibh Dia,
Le haltughadh 'sro-ghairdeachas
'sna hairdibh, molfaibh 'nTriath.
2. Uil' aingle, molfalbh e a gcian:
is uile shluagh nach gann:
3. Gloir tabhraibh, gealach dho is grian
'sgach reulla soluis ann.
4. A neamh' na neamha molfaidh e:
'sgach uifg' osciond na nspeur.
5. Ard-mheanmnach an ainm Dhe
O biodh iad gu leir.
Ar gcur da orduigh uaidh amach
ghrad chruthuigheadh gach ni.
6. Rinn reachd is teilgin nach dteid thart:
is shocruigh iad a chaoich.
^. O thalmhuin molfaibh Dia do ghna,
gach dragun, doimhn', is tuil.
^. Tein' is cloch-shneachd, gaillion 'sgach gal
sion-chath-ghaoi, rinn a thoil.
^. A bheanntaidh, is a chnoctha feoir,
gach cedar is craobh-meas.
^0. Gach eallach, is gach ainmhidh mhor,
snamhaich, is cunlaith deas.
^1. Gach righ ar talmhuin, is gach sluagh,
prionnsa, 'sgach britheamh naomh.
12. Gach oganach, 'sgach ainnir bhreagh,
sean-daoin' is clanna mhaodh.
13. Fior-mholfaid ainm Dhe gu mor:
oir ainm amhain ata
To oirdheirc onorach: a ghloir
thar neamh is lar gu brath.
14. Se thogbhas adharc a phobuil suas*
sud clu a naoimh gu leir,
Siol Israel, sluagh theann se ris.
O molfaibh Dia le cheil.
SALM CXLIX.
DEagh-chantuireachd ro-bhuaghach ard
sinnibh do Dhia le clu,
Gu fonnmhur oran canfaidh dho
a ngcoimhthional na naomh.
2. Gu fursailteach biodh Israel
'sa nti do chruthaigh e;
Gu luthghaireach biodh Sion fos
na righ roi-dhileas feign.
3. Ainm Dhe san damhsa molfadh iad
le tiombain is le cruit.
4. Oir gabhaidh Dia de^ghthoil da shluagh,
iad chi a shuil, gu hait:
Deagh-mhaisighidh le slainte, e,
na daoine suairce seimh.
5. Ard-cheol na nleapthaibh deanadh iad
'sbiodh ait a ngloir, na naoimh.
6. Na mbeil ard-mholadh Dhe, sna nl^imh
cloidhimh faobharthach gach taobh:
Air gheinntleach thabhairt dioghaltas,
is smachd ar phobal baodh;
8. Do chum a nrighthe chuibhriughadh
le slamhradhaibh gu teann,
An ro-dhaoin' is an jarladha
le geimhlibh jaruinn bhuan.
9. Chur orr' a bhreathamhnas a ngniomh
mar sgriobht' ata gu ceart:
Sud onoir gheibh a naoimh gu leir.
O molfaidh Dia na mfeart.
SASM CL.
O Taibhraibh clu do Dhia na gloir.
Mol e na jonad naomh:
'An fhiormaintibh a chumhachd mhoir
molfaibh an Triath gu caomh.
2. Arson a ghniomhartha to thren
bibh ait a nDia na ndul.
Reir feabhas fos a mhordhachd feign
bibh binn do, ann sgach jul.
3. Le fuaim na sduice, molfaibh e,
le clarsigh 's adhbhuidh civil.
9. Le tiombain, pioba, forgainn bhreagh,
's le hinnil teudadh-caol.
5. Air chiomboil chluigneach deanuibh ceol:
air bhonnain fhuaimneach ard.
6. Gach ni fuair anail, molfadh dho.
Sior-mholfaibh Dia began chaird.
FOIRCHIOND.
Is sgiursa ar dheamhnaibh, duine
ar fiuchadh le crabhadh.
CAINTIC SHIMEOIN a S. Lucais Caibidil 2. Rann. 29. etc.
ADHE, do leigfais nois ga chlos
do d'shearbhont dol a nsith
Do reir na geallaidh fuair me bhos
mar rabhadh uait, mo righ.
2, Oir Feuch, do chonnaic mo dha shul
neach thugfais duinn mar shlaint'
3. Do dheasuigh thu, is chuir na evil
a nlathair saluaigh gach caint'
4. Chum by na sholas dealrach glan
do gheinntiligh le cheil
Da mfoilsiugb^dh; 'sna ghloir gu buan
do dphobal Israel.
Caintic le SACHARIAS a S. Lucais C. 1, v. 68. etc.
BEANNUIGHT' gu ^aibh Dia Israel
dfhiosruigh a phobal feign:
Oir fhuasgail se o neigin iad,
'so nuile pheacadh geur.
2. Adharc-shlanaigh thog se, air ar son
a ntigh a Dhaibhidh feign.
3. Mar labhair trid a fhaighibh naomh
o thus an domhain, e.
4. Gu saoradh se or' naimhdibh sin
'so dhaoin' a nmiorunn rinn,
5. Thoirt jochd, mar ghoall dar' naithreacha,
'sa chumhnant naomh, gu cuimhn'.
6. An mhoid do thug se dh Abraham,
7. Gu deonuigheadh e dhuinn
Deis saoradh o ar naimhdibh garg.
gu g^bhadh seirbhis uainn,
Do dheanamaoid began eagal, do.
8. An naomhachd is a nceart
Gach la dar mbeathaidh is dar saoghail
na fhiaghnais feign, gu hait.
9. Is tussa, naoidh, se ainm bhias duit,
faigh ud an ti is aird:
Roimh ghnuis a nTighe^rn' theid thu suas,
'sa jul ni deas began chaird.
10. Da phobal bheir tu ciall na slaint',
thaoibh maitheamhnas na nlochd.
11. Trid throcair chaomh ar nDia 'sar righ
a sholas duinn do nochd,
Ceud ga na greine is an lo
do eirigh oirn on aird,
12. Thoirt solas do na shuigh san dorch'
'sa ndubhar bhais bhi baitht,
Do threorughadh gach bail a mbi
ar geosa chaoich, 'sar ceim,
An jul na sithchaimh is na slaint',
'sdar seoladh jonnt' leis feign.
CAINTIC MHUIRE an tsior-oighe. a Soisgeil Lucais Caib. 1. R. 46. etc.
GHABH manam nois ma mhordhachd Dhe,
cuirfim a chlu agceill.
2. Is rinn mo Spiorad gairdeachus
a nDia mo shlanaigheoir feign.
3. Oir isle staid a bhanoglaigh
do thug fanear, mo righ,
Oir feuch o so amach, gach aois
their siad gur beannuight me.
4, Oir rinn an ti 'ta neartmhur caomh
mor-neithe dhamh began cheist
Ro-naomh ata a ainm gu brath.
5. Da bhuil a throcair deas
Is grasa da luchd eagail feign
o linn amach do linn.
6. Le ban a ridheadh nochd se neart,
is sgaoil e feign gu cinnt'
Na daoine uaibhreach, ailghiosach,
'sgach beairt do dheilbh a ngcroidh.
7. O ngcathaoiribh do leag e sios
an gcumhachdach, gach ti,
Lion a nlag inimhe ata
siad sin a dharduigh Dia.
8. Daoin 'ocrach lion le neithibh maith
chuir saidhbhir folamh uaidh.
9. A shearbhont Israil chuidigh se,
chuimhnigh a throcair glan.
10. Mar labhair se dar naithreacha,
d'Abram, 'sda shiol gu buan.
An Ghloir-bhriathar.
GLoir o gach neach do Dhia, an athar
dan' Mhic, 'sdo nSpioraid naoimh;
Mar bhi o thus, is nois ata,
mar bhios fos a chaoich.
An Ghloir-bhriathar, a nos an dara
udhaim Mhiodarrachd don' 136. Psalm.
Buan-ghloir don' athair chaoimh
Is don' Mhie mhaisigh mhin;
Beirmid don Spioraid naoimh
Comhmeas an ghloir sin feign:
Mar bhi, sul chum
Dia mor gach ni,
'Ta, is bhias ann
Began cheann began chrich.
